  dplyr::left_join(pCPI, by = "year")

# ---------------------------
# REBASE TO 2010 = 100
# ---------------------------

rebase_to_2010 <- function(x, year, base_year = 2010) {
  base_val <- x[year == base_year]
  if (length(base_val) == 0 || is.na(base_val)) return(x)
  return(100 * x / base_val)
}

prices <- prices |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    dplyr::across(
      c(pY, pC, pG, pK, pX, pM, pTI, wp, pCPI),
      ~ rebase_to_2010(.x, year)
    )
  )

Thought for 45s
Yes. These are the right two fires to put out first 🔧

On the first one, the problem is real and it is not cosmetic. Your own session note already states the mismatch clearly: the successful exporter followed the saved bundle tied to ln_r_diag_t, while the core had already switched the turning-point search upstream to ln_r_struct_t; then pruning/finalization still used xvar = "ln_r_diag_t". That means the run “worked” only because search and final object assembly were borrowing from two different profit-rate objects. 


What has to happen is simple: the builder must use one and only one swing carrier from end to end. Search, prune, finalize, classify, label, and export all need to reference the same series. No hybrids. The clean rule is:

if the interpretive object is the structurally filtered profit rate, then everything downstream should use ln_r_struct_t

if the interpretive object is the diagnostic/raw-smoothed rate, then everything downstream should use ln_r_diag_t

Given your current architecture, I would freeze the builder on ln_r_struct_t and make the exporter inherit that from the bundle metadata instead of hard-coding a series name. The bug is not just “drift”; it changes what counts as a peak, what counts as a trough, and therefore what counts as a historical phase.

The repair I’d make in the core is this pattern:

swing_xvar <- "ln_r_struct_t"   # single source of truth

tp_candidates <- detect_turning_points(
  data = swings_df,
  xvar = swing_xvar,
  year_var = "year",
  ...
)

tp_pruned <- prune_turning_points(
  data = swings_df,
  tp = tp_candidates,
  xvar = swing_xvar,
  year_var = "year",
  ...
)

tp_env_final <- finalize_turning_points(
  data = swings_df,
  tp = tp_pruned,
  xvar = swing_xvar,
  year_var = "year",
  ...
)

bundle$profit_swings <- list(
  xvar = swing_xvar,
  tp_env_final = tp_env_final,
  ...
)
Then in the exporter:

stopifnot(!is.null(bundle$profit_swings$xvar))
swing_xvar <- bundle$profit_swings$xvar
tp_env_final <- bundle$profit_swings$tp_env_final
That eliminates the “future intended variant / past saved bundle” split. Right now the exporter is being disciplined by the bundle, but the bundle itself still carries a conceptual impurity.

Now the second issue is even more important substantively. If the swing algorithm is carving the Chile series in a way that obliterates the Unidad Popular as crisis, then the turning-point routine is overfitting local extrema and underfitting historical sequence. Your own historical framing is very explicit: the UP is a bounded political project from 1970–1973, while the fall/crisis concentrates especially in 1972–1973, and the late 1960s already register an ISI impasse that prepares that rupture. 


So the audit question is not “did the algorithm find mathematically valid local turning points?” The question is:

Does the detected swing structure preserve the historically meaningful sequence
late-1960s impasse → UP attempt (1970–71) → acute crisis/dislocation (1972–73) → post-coup reorganization?

If not, then the algorithm is too eager.

My suspicion is that one or more of these is happening:

First, the minimum phase length is too short. That lets the 1970–1973 years get chopped into tiny peak-trough-peak fragments, which is fatal in annual data.

Second, the prominence threshold is too low, so transitory reversals inside the UP years are being promoted into full regime swings.

Third, the algorithm probably treats all turning points symmetrically, when in your case 1972–1973 should be allowed to emerge as an acute crisis descent even if a short-lived rebound exists inside the interval.

So I would audit the builder in exactly this order.

Start by printing the raw candidate turning points for 1965–1976 only. Not the final table. The raw candidates. You want to see which local extrema are being generated before pruning.

Then print the pruned table with these fields only:
tp_id, year, type, x_level, prominence, left_span, right_span

Then print the finalized swings:
start_year, end_year, direction, peak_year, trough_year, amplitude

That alone usually exposes the crime scene 😄

For annual Chile data, I would impose three historical guardrails.

One, minimum complete swing length of 3 years, preferably 4 for contraction/expansion segmentation.

Two, no two turning points closer than 2 years unless the second dominates the first in absolute amplitude.

Three, a historical anchor rule for 1970–1973: internal reversals inside that interval can be kept as annotations, but they should not automatically split the main crisis sequence unless the amplitude exceeds a high override threshold.

In pseudo-logic:

is_up_window <- function(y) y >= 1970 & y <= 1973

tp_pruned <- tp_candidates |>
  enforce_min_gap(min_gap = 2) |>
  enforce_min_phase_length(min_years = 3) |>
  enforce_prominence(min_prom = base_prom)

tp_pruned <- preserve_historical_window(
  tp = tp_pruned,
  years = 1970:1973,
  split_only_if = \(amp, prom) amp >= up_override_amp && prom >= up_override_prom
)
That does not “hard-code history” in a crude way. It stops the algorithm from shredding a historically unified crisis interval because of small local noise.

Substantively, I would recommend this target periodization for the profit-swing audit, not yet as final output but as the benchmark you test against:

1967/68–1970: late ISI impasse / pre-UP deterioration

1970–1971: UP initial expansionary or attempted recovery phase

1971/72–1973: acute crisis sequence

1973–1975/76: coercive reorganization / aftermath

That structure is consistent with your own long-duration framing of Chilean accumulation crisis and with the specific concentration of the fall in 1972–1973. 


So my recommendation is:

First, unify the swing carrier in the builder and exporter around one xvar, ideally ln_r_struct_t.

Second, rerun the turning-point audit only for 1965–1976 with a diagnostic table of candidates, pruned points, and finalized swings.

Third, tighten the pruning rules so the UP interval is not fragmented by minor internal reversals.

Fourth, only after that regenerate the period labels and narrative tables.

The key principle is this: in your setup, profit swings are not just descriptive oscillations. They are periodizing devices. If the device destroys the historical object it is supposed to clarify, the device is misspecified.

Paste the turning-point section of the builder here and I’ll rewrite it line by line into a historically disciplined version.

for the case of the US we decided that the algorithm to identify profit swings was driven by the shift on the first difference of a smoothed profit rate 

here is the code, we need to build consistency in the comparative analysis, but also calibrate for historical coherence 

# ── 6. Turning-point helpers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
find_turning_points_direction <- function(year, x, k = 3) {
  dx <- x - dplyr::lag(x)
  dx_ma <- zoo::rollmean(dx, k = k, fill = NA, align = "center")
  
  out <- vector("list", 0)
  for (i in 2:(length(dx_ma) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(dx_ma[i - 1]) || is.na(dx_ma[i])) next
    if (dx_ma[i - 1] > 0 && dx_ma[i] < 0) {
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(idx = i, year = year[i], value = x[i], type = "peak")
    } else if (dx_ma[i - 1] < 0 && dx_ma[i] > 0) {
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(idx = i, year = year[i], value = x[i], type = "trough")
    }
  }
  
  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(idx = integer(), year = integer(), value = numeric(), type = character()))
  }
  
  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |> dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

compress_turning_points <- function(tp) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)
  
  keep <- vector("list", 0)
  current <- tp[1, , drop = FALSE]
  
  for (i in 2:nrow(tp)) {
    this <- tp[i, , drop = FALSE]
    if (this$type == current$type) {
      if (this$type == "peak" && this$value > current$value) current <- this
      if (this$type == "trough" && this$value < current$value) current <- this
    } else {
      keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
      current <- this
    }
  }
  
  keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
  dplyr::bind_rows(keep) |> dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

prune_turning_points <- function(tp, x, min_move = 0.10, min_years = 3) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)
  out <- tp
  
  repeat {
    if (nrow(out) <= 1) break
    
    amp <- abs(diff(x[out$idx]))
    dur <- diff(out$year)
    weak <- which(amp < min_move | dur < min_years)
    if (length(weak) == 0) break
    
    k <- weak[1]
    
    if (k == 1) {
      out <- out[-2, , drop = FALSE]
    } else if (k == nrow(out) - 1) {
      out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
    } else {
      left_idx  <- out$idx[k - 1]
      a_idx     <- out$idx[k]
      b_idx     <- out$idx[k + 1]
      right_idx <- out$idx[k + 2]
      
      move_drop_left  <- abs(x[b_idx] - x[left_idx])
      move_drop_right <- abs(x[right_idx] - x[a_idx])
      
      if (move_drop_left >= move_drop_right) {
        out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
      } else {
        out <- out[-(k + 1), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }
    
    out <- compress_turning_points(out)
  }
  
  out
}

prune_turning_points_windowed <- function(tp, data, xvar,
                                          war_end = 1946,
                                          min_move_war = 0.08,
                                          min_years_war = 2,
                                          min_move_post = 0.10,
                                          min_years_post = 3) {
  tp_war  <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year <= war_end)
  tp_post <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year >= war_end)
  
  tp_war_pruned <- if (nrow(tp_war) > 0) {
    tp_war |>
      compress_turning_points() |>
      prune_turning_points(x = data[[xvar]], min_move = min_move_war, min_years = min_years_war)
  } else tp_war
  
  tp_post_pruned <- if (nrow(tp_post) > 0) {
    tp_post |>
      compress_turning_points() |>
      prune_turning_points(x = data[[xvar]], min_move = min_move_post, min_years = min_years_post)
  } else tp_post
  
  dplyr::bind_rows(tp_war_pruned, tp_post_pruned) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

drop_weak_terminal_swing <- function(tp, data, xvar, min_years = 3, min_move = 0.02) {
  if (nrow(tp) < 2) return(tp)
  
  dur_last <- tp$year[nrow(tp)] - tp$year[nrow(tp) - 1]
  amp_last <- abs(data[[xvar]][tp$idx[nrow(tp)]] - data[[xvar]][tp$idx[nrow(tp) - 1]])
  
  if (dur_last < min_years && amp_last < min_move) {
    tp <- tp[-nrow(tp), , drop = FALSE]
  }
  
  tp
}

add_boundaries <- function(tp, data, xvar) {
  if (nrow(tp) == 0) stop("No internal turning points detected.")
  
  first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  
  start_row <- tibble::tibble(
    idx = 1,
    year = data$year[1],
    value = data[[xvar]][1],
    type = first_type
  )
  
  end_row <- tibble::tibble(
    idx = nrow(data),
    year = data$year[nrow(data)],
    value = data[[xvar]][nrow(data)],
    type = last_type
  )
  
  dplyr::bind_rows(start_row, tp, end_row) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

Thought for 15s
Yes — now we’re at the real methodological knot 🧩

The issue is not only “consistency with the US.” It is that the current routine, as written, can easily produce historically displaced turning points, especially around short, dense crisis intervals like 1969–1974 in Chile.

Your code is elegant, but it has four features that can distort periodization.

First, the turning point is triggered by a sign change in a centered moving average of first differences:

dx <- x - dplyr::lag(x)
dx_ma <- zoo::rollmean(dx, k = k, fill = NA, align = "center")
That means the signal for year i uses information from both sides of i. In annual data, with k = 3, this can shift the apparent turning point by about one year. For the Unidad Popular sequence, that is huge. A crisis concentrated in 1972–1973 can get represented as a peak in 1972 and a trough in 1974, which is exactly the kind of historical slippage that makes the UP crisis disappear into the post-coup aftermath.

Second, the algorithm detects the reversal on the smoothed derivative, but stores the turning point at:

year = year[i], value = x[i]
So the dating of the turning point is inherited mechanically from the sign-change index, not from the actual local extremum in x. That is a second source of drift.

Third, the pruning is done on amplitude and duration in the level of x, but the detection is done on dx_ma. That can be fine, but only if the same carrier series is used throughout. If detection is on one object and pruning/finalization on another, the dating becomes conceptually incoherent.

Fourth, add_boundaries() forces artificial endpoints:

first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
That is convenient for plotting complete swings, but it can create pseudo-swings at the start and end of the sample that look more “objective” than they really are.

So the main diagnosis is this:

your current method is not just smoothing noise; it is also capable of relocating crisis chronology.

That is why the UP gets flattened.

The image you shared shows exactly that pathology. The series appears to crest around 1972, then fall to a trough around 1974, with a recovery after that. But historically, for your interpretive purpose, the critical question is whether the profit crisis is being read as:

a crisis inside the Unidad Popular sequence, or

a crisis that begins only after it.

Those are not the same historical story.

Here is the clean repair path.

The comparative rule can still be retained:

turning points are triggered by reversals in the first difference of a smoothed profit-rate series

But for Chile, historical coherence requires an additional rule:

the date of each turning point should be assigned to the actual local extremum of x within a short neighborhood around the derivative sign change, not automatically to the sign-change year itself.

That fixes a lot.

In practice, you want detection and dating separated:

detect candidate reversals from smoothed Δx

for each candidate, search in a small neighborhood of x — say i-1:i+1 or i-2:i+2

assign the turning point to the actual max/min year in that neighborhood

So instead of:

if (dx_ma[i - 1] > 0 && dx_ma[i] < 0) {
  tibble(idx = i, year = year[i], value = x[i], type = "peak")
}
you want something like:

locate_local_extremum <- function(year, x, i, type, span = 1) {
  lo <- max(1, i - span)
  hi <- min(length(x), i + span)
  window_idx <- lo:hi
  
  j <- if (type == "peak") {
    window_idx[which.max(x[window_idx])]
  } else {
    window_idx[which.min(x[window_idx])]
  }
  
  tibble::tibble(idx = j, year = year[j], value = x[j], type = type)
}
and then in detection:

if (dx_ma[i - 1] > 0 && dx_ma[i] < 0) {
  out[[length(out) + 1]] <- locate_local_extremum(year, x, i, "peak", span = 1)
} else if (dx_ma[i - 1] < 0 && dx_ma[i] > 0) {
  out[[length(out) + 1]] <- locate_local_extremum(year, x, i, "trough", span = 1)
}
That preserves the US logic while avoiding the “1972 signal dated as 1974 consequence” problem.

There is also a small bug-like inconsistency in the windowed pruning:

tp_war  <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year <= war_end)
tp_post <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year >= war_end)
This duplicates war_end into both subsets. You later distinct() it away, so it may not explode, but it is sloppy. It should be:

tp_post <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year > war_end)
Now, on calibration for historical coherence, I would not use the exact same thresholds for Chile that you used for the US without adjustment. Not because Chile should be “hand-held,” but because annual Chile data over 1940–1978 contains a much denser political-economic break structure. You need the algorithm to avoid overfragmentation, but also to preserve the UP crisis as a bounded episode.

I would calibrate Chile with three principles.

First, use the same detection logic as the US, but assign dates via local extrema.

Second, use a slightly stricter minimum duration in the late sample, especially for 1965 onward. For annual data, min_years = 3 is reasonable, but if the routine is still fragmenting 1970–1974, push it to 4 for finalized historical periodization and keep the looser version only for diagnostics.

Third, do not let minor reversals inside 1970–1973 automatically split the main crisis sequence. The UP period should only be split internally if the amplitude is substantively large. Otherwise those local movements should be annotations, not separate major swings.

Conceptually, I’d distinguish two layers:

diagnostic turning points: every mathematically plausible reversal

historical major swings: pruned sequence used for periodization

That way you do not suppress data; you just stop confusing noise or short internal oscillations with major historical phases.

So I would rewrite your helpers into two-stage logic:

find_turning_points_direction() → diagnostic candidates

prune_turning_points_historical() → major swing sequence

And in the historical pruner, add an optional protected window:

prune_turning_points_historical <- function(tp, x, min_move = 0.10, min_years = 3,
                                            protect_window = NULL,
                                            protect_override_move = 0.15) {
  ...
}
where protect_window = c(1970, 1973) means:
inside that interval, do not split into multiple major swings unless amplitude exceeds protect_override_move.

One more thing: if x is indeed a log profit rate, min_move = 0.10 is not absurd. If x is the level profit rate, it is enormous. So the thresholds must be tied explicitly to the carrier. That needs to be frozen in metadata. No more silent ambiguity.

My recommendation is this exact comparative rule:

detection carrier: smoothed Δ ln r_struct

dating rule: local extremum of ln r_struct

pruning carrier: ln r_struct

historical major-swing thresholds: country-specific but declared

endpoint boundaries: only for plotting, never for inferential periodization tables

That last part matters. add_boundaries() should feed figures, not period classification.

So the repair package is:

unify the swing carrier

separate detection from dating

fix the overlapping window split

distinguish diagnostic vs historical swings

demote forced boundaries to plotting only

add a protected historical calibration for 1970–1973 in Chile

If you want, next I’ll give you a fully rewritten block of these helper functions in R, keeping your architecture but making the Chile/US comparison methodologically consistent and historically sane.

Perfect—this clarifies the target much more sharply 🎯

You’re not asking the algorithm to respect a date.
You’re asking it to recover a sequence of structural movements:

breakdown → partial offset → reversal → forced offset → exhaustion

That’s a completely different constraint than “don’t split 1970–73.”

Let’s lock that properly and translate it into code logic.

1. What your current algorithm is missing
Right now your routine is purely local:

detects sign flips in smoothed Δx

prunes by amplitude + duration

compresses alternating extrema

This means:

it sees oscillations, not processes

So it cannot distinguish between:

a minor rebound
vs

a historically meaningful offset phase

That’s exactly why your UP sequence gets flattened.

2. Your target structure (formalized)
Let’s rewrite your historical expectation in signal terms:

Desired pattern in ln r_struct_t
Late 60s → declining trend (dysfunction buildup)

1971 → strong positive impulse (offsetting)

1972–73 → reversal (renewed decline)

Post-73 → strong positive impulse (forced offsetting)

Late period → weakening / unsustained recovery

So the algorithm must detect not just:

turning points

but:

clusters of directional persistence

3. Minimal fix (do NOT redesign everything)
We keep your architecture. We add one layer:

👉 classify swings by cumulative directional movement, not just endpoints

4. Critical upgrade: directional runs
Add this AFTER turning points are finalized.

Step 1: build directional segments
build_directional_runs <- function(data, xvar) {
  dx <- diff(data[[xvar]])
  sign_dx <- sign(dx)
  
  runs <- rle(sign_dx)
  
  out <- vector("list", length(runs$lengths))
  idx_start <- 1
  
  for (i in seq_along(runs$lengths)) {
    len <- runs$lengths[i]
    sgn <- runs$values[i]
    
    idx_end <- idx_start + len
    
    out[[i]] <- tibble::tibble(
      start_year = data$year[idx_start],
      end_year   = data$year[idx_end],
      direction  = sgn,
      duration   = len,
      cum_move   = sum(dx[idx_start:(idx_end - 1)], na.rm = TRUE)
    )
    
    idx_start <- idx_end
  }
  
  dplyr::bind_rows(out)
}
Step 2: classify runs
classify_runs <- function(runs, big_move = 0.08) {
  runs |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      phase = dplyr::case_when(
        direction > 0 & cum_move >  big_move ~ "strong_offset",
        direction > 0                        ~ "weak_offset",
        direction < 0 & cum_move < -big_move ~ "strong_decline",
        direction < 0                        ~ "weak_decline",
        TRUE ~ "flat"
      )
    )
}

“there was a peak in 1972 and a trough in 1974”

1971–1973 → strong_decline

1973–1975 → strong_offset

1975–1978 → weak_offset / weakening

🔥 That’s exactly your historical narrative.

bundle$profit_runs <- runs_classified

# ── 2. Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
stop_missing <- function(path) {
  if (!file.exists(path)) stop("Required file not found: ", path, call. = FALSE)
}

read_any <- function(path) {
  ext <- tolower(tools::file_ext(path))
  if (ext == "csv") return(readr::read_csv(path, show_col_types = FALSE))
  if (ext == "rds") return(readRDS(path))
  stop("Unsupported extension for: ", path, call. = FALSE)
}

find_first_present <- function(df, candidates, what) {
  hit <- intersect(candidates, names(df))
  if (length(hit) == 0) {
    stop(
      "Could not identify ", what,
      ". Candidates checked: ", paste(candidates, collapse = ", "),
      call. = FALSE
    )
  }
  hit[1]
}

rename_first <- function(df, candidates, new_name, what = new_name) {
  old <- find_first_present(df, candidates, what)
  dplyr::rename(df, !!new_name := !!rlang::sym(old))
}

first_non_na <- function(x) {
  y <- x[!is.na(x)]
  if (length(y) == 0) return(NA_real_)
  y[1]
}

last_non_na <- function(x) {
  y <- x[!is.na(x)]
  if (length(y) == 0) return(NA_real_)
  y[length(y)]
}

extract_stage1_ect <- function(stage1_master, sample, spec = "S1_B", lag = 1, rank = 1) {
  out <- stage1_master$ect_series |>
    dplyr::filter(sample == !!sample, spec == !!spec, lag == !!lag, rank == !!rank) |>
    dplyr::arrange(year) |>
    dplyr::select(year, ECT)

  if (nrow(out) == 0) {
    stop(
      "No Stage 1 ECT found for sample=", sample,
      ", spec=", spec, ", lag=", lag, ", rank=", rank,
      call. = FALSE
    )
  }

  out
}

rescue_u_path <- function(df, pinch_year = 1980L) {
  df <- df |> dplyr::arrange(year)
  idx0 <- which(df$year == pinch_year)
  if (length(idx0) != 1L) stop("Pinch year not found uniquely in splice panel.", call. = FALSE)

  logYp <- rep(NA_real_, nrow(df))
  logYp[idx0] <- df$y[idx0]

  if (idx0 < nrow(df)) {
    for (i in (idx0 + 1):nrow(df)) {
      if (!is.finite(df$dlog_k_nr[i]) || !is.finite(df$theta_active[i])) {
        stop("Missing dlog_k_nr or theta_active in forward recursion at year ", df$year[i], call. = FALSE)
      }
      logYp[i] <- logYp[i - 1] + df$theta_active[i] * df$dlog_k_nr[i]
    }
  }

  if (idx0 > 1) {
    for (i in seq(idx0 - 1, 1)) {
      j <- i + 1
      if (!is.finite(df$dlog_k_nr[j]) || !is.finite(df$theta_active[j])) {
        stop("Missing dlog_k_nr or theta_active in backward recursion at year ", df$year[j], call. = FALSE)
      }
      logYp[i] <- logYp[j] - df$theta_active[j] * df$dlog_k_nr[j]
    }
  }

  df |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      log_y_p = logYp,
      y_p = exp(log_y_p),
      mu_t = exp(y - log_y_p)
    )
}

sign_eps <- function(x, eps = 1e-10) {
  ifelse(abs(x) <= eps | is.na(x), 0L, ifelse(x > 0, 1L, -1L))
}

locate_local_extremum <- function(year, x, i, type, span = 1L) {
  lo <- max(1L, i - span)
  hi <- min(length(x), i + span)
  window_idx <- lo:hi
  window_x <- x[window_idx]

  if (all(is.na(window_x))) {
    return(tibble::tibble(idx = i, year = year[i], value = x[i], type = type))
  }

  j <- if (type == "peak") {
    window_idx[which.max(window_x)]
  } else {
    window_idx[which.min(window_x)]
  }

  tibble::tibble(idx = j, year = year[j], value = x[j], type = type)
}

find_turning_points_direction <- function(year, x, k = 3L, span = 1L, eps = 1e-10) {
  dx <- x - dplyr::lag(x)
  dx_ma <- zoo::rollmean(dx, k = k, fill = NA, align = "center")

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  for (i in 2:(length(dx_ma) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(dx_ma[i - 1]) || is.na(dx_ma[i])) next

    prev_s <- sign_eps(dx_ma[i - 1], eps = eps)
    curr_s <- sign_eps(dx_ma[i], eps = eps)

    if (prev_s > 0L && curr_s < 0L) {
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- locate_local_extremum(year, x, i, "peak", span = span)
    } else if (prev_s < 0L && curr_s > 0L) {
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- locate_local_extremum(year, x, i, "trough", span = span)
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

compress_turning_points <- function(tp) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  keep <- vector("list", 0)
  current <- tp[1, , drop = FALSE]

  for (i in 2:nrow(tp)) {
    this <- tp[i, , drop = FALSE]

    if (this$type == current$type) {
      if (this$type == "peak" && this$value > current$value) current <- this
      if (this$type == "trough" && this$value < current$value) current <- this
    } else {
      keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
      current <- this
    }
  }

  keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current

  dplyr::bind_rows(keep) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

prune_turning_points <- function(tp, x, min_move = 0.10, min_years = 3) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  out <- tp

  repeat {
    if (nrow(out) <= 1) break

    amp <- abs(diff(x[out$idx]))
    dur <- diff(out$year)
    weak <- which(amp < min_move | dur < min_years)

    if (length(weak) == 0) break

    k <- weak[1]

    if (k == 1) {
      out <- out[-2, , drop = FALSE]
    } else if (k == nrow(out) - 1) {
      out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
    } else {
      left_idx  <- out$idx[k - 1]
      a_idx     <- out$idx[k]
      b_idx     <- out$idx[k + 1]
      right_idx <- out$idx[k + 2]

      move_drop_left  <- abs(x[b_idx] - x[left_idx])
      move_drop_right <- abs(x[right_idx] - x[a_idx])

      if (move_drop_left >= move_drop_right) {
        out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
      } else {
        out <- out[-(k + 1), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }

    out <- compress_turning_points(out)
  }

  out
}

prune_turning_points_windowed <- function(tp, data, xvar,
                                          break_year = 1946,
                                          min_move_early = 0.08,
                                          min_years_early = 2,
                                          min_move_late = 0.10,
                                          min_years_late = 3) {
  tp_early <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year <= break_year)
  tp_late  <- tp |> dplyr::filter(year > break_year)

  tp_early_pruned <- if (nrow(tp_early) > 0) {
    tp_early |>
      compress_turning_points() |>
      prune_turning_points(
        x = data[[xvar]],
        min_move = min_move_early,
        min_years = min_years_early
      )
  } else {
    tp_early
  }

  tp_late_pruned <- if (nrow(tp_late) > 0) {
    tp_late |>
      compress_turning_points() |>
      prune_turning_points(
        x = data[[xvar]],
        min_move = min_move_late,
        min_years = min_years_late
      )
  } else {
    tp_late
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(tp_early_pruned, tp_late_pruned) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

add_boundaries_for_plot <- function(tp, data, xvar) {
  if (nrow(tp) == 0) stop("No internal turning points detected.", call. = FALSE)

  first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"

  start_row <- tibble::tibble(
    idx = 1L,
    year = data$year[1],
    value = data[[xvar]][1],
    type = first_type
  )

  end_row <- tibble::tibble(
    idx = nrow(data),
    year = data$year[nrow(data)],
    value = data[[xvar]][nrow(data)],
    type = last_type
  )

  dplyr::bind_rows(start_row, tp, end_row) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

drop_weak_terminal_swing <- function(tp, data, xvar, min_years = 3, min_move = 0.02) {
  if (nrow(tp) < 2) return(tp)

  dur_last <- tp$year[nrow(tp)] - tp$year[nrow(tp) - 1]
  amp_last <- abs(data[[xvar]][tp$idx[nrow(tp)]] - data[[xvar]][tp$idx[nrow(tp) - 1]])

  if (dur_last < min_years && amp_last < min_move) {
    tp <- tp[-nrow(tp), , drop = FALSE]
  }

  tp
}

build_swing_table <- function(tp, data) {
  if (nrow(tp) < 2) return(tibble::tibble())

  out <- vector("list", nrow(tp) - 1)

  for (i in 1:(nrow(tp) - 1)) {
    start_idx <- tp$idx[i]
    end_idx   <- tp$idx[i + 1]

    start_year <- tp$year[i]
    end_year   <- tp$year[i + 1]
    dur <- end_year - start_year

    start_r_diag <- data$r_diag_t[start_idx]
    end_r_diag   <- data$r_diag_t[end_idx]

    start_ln_struct <- data$ln_r_struct_t[start_idx]
    end_ln_struct   <- data$ln_r_struct_t[end_idx]
    amp_log_struct  <- end_ln_struct - start_ln_struct

    out[[i]] <- tibble::tibble(
      swing_id = i,
      start_year = start_year,
      end_year = end_year,
      direction = paste0(tp$type[i], "_to_", tp$type[i + 1]),
      duration_years = dur,
      start_r_diag = start_r_diag,
      end_r_diag = end_r_diag,
      amplitude_pct_diag = 100 * (end_r_diag / start_r_diag - 1),
      pace_pct_diag_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, 100 * ((end_r_diag / start_r_diag)^(1 / dur) - 1), NA_real_),
      amplitude_log_struct = amp_log_struct,
      pace_log_struct_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, amp_log_struct / dur, NA_real_)
    )
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out)
}

add_swing_decomposition <- function(swing_tbl, tp, data) {
  out <- swing_tbl
  comps <- c("dist", "util", "price", "capacity", "wedge")

  for (nm in comps) out[[paste0(nm, "_log")]] <- NA_real_
  out$total_log_check <- NA_real_
  for (nm in comps) out[[paste0(nm, "_share_pct")]] <- NA_real_
  out$share_sum_pct <- NA_real_

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(out))) {
    start_idx <- tp$idx[i]
    end_idx   <- tp$idx[i + 1]

    d_pi <- data$ln_pi_t[end_idx] - data$ln_pi_t[start_idx]
    d_mu <- data$ln_mu_t[end_idx] - data$ln_mu_t[start_idx]
    d_p  <- data$ln_p_t[end_idx]  - data$ln_p_t[start_idx]
    d_B  <- data$ln_B_t[end_idx]  - data$ln_B_t[start_idx]
    d_nu <- data$ln_nu_t[end_idx] - data$ln_nu_t[start_idx]
    d_r  <- out$amplitude_log_struct[i]

    vals <- c(dist = d_pi, util = d_mu, price = d_p, capacity = d_B, wedge = d_nu)

    for (nm in names(vals)) out[[paste0(nm, "_log")]][i] <- vals[[nm]]
    out$total_log_check[i] <- sum(vals)

    if (!is.na(d_r) && abs(d_r) > 1e-10) {
      for (nm in names(vals)) out[[paste0(nm, "_share_pct")]][i] <- 100 * vals[[nm]] / d_r
      out$share_sum_pct[i] <- 100 * sum(vals) / d_r
    }
  }

  out
}

add_swing_indices <- function(swing_tbl, eps = 1e-10) {
  out <- swing_tbl
  out$G_swing <- NA_real_
  out$N_swing <- NA_real_
  out$D_swing <- NA_real_
  out$O_swing <- NA_real_
  out$S_off_swing <- NA_real_
  out$F_rev_swing <- NA_real_

  comp_cols <- c("dist_log", "util_log", "price_log", "capacity_log", "wedge_log")

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(out))) {
    comps <- as.numeric(out[i, comp_cols])
    G <- sum(abs(comps), na.rm = TRUE)
    N <- sum(comps, na.rm = TRUE)
    sgn <- sign_eps(N, eps = eps)
    O <- if (sgn == 0L) G else sum(abs(comps[sign_eps(comps, eps = eps) == -sgn]), na.rm = TRUE)

    out$G_swing[i] <- G
    out$N_swing[i] <- N
    out$D_swing[i] <- ifelse(G > eps, 1 - abs(N) / G, NA_real_)
    out$O_swing[i] <- O
    out$S_off_swing[i] <- ifelse(G > eps, O / G, NA_real_)
    out$F_rev_swing[i] <- ifelse((O + abs(N)) > eps, O / (O + abs(N)), NA_real_)
  }

  out
}

classify_swing_phase <- function(swing_tbl, major_move = 0.08) {
  if (nrow(swing_tbl) == 0) return(swing_tbl)

  swing_tbl |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      direction_sign = dplyr::case_when(
        direction == "trough_to_peak" ~ 1L,
        direction == "peak_to_trough" ~ -1L,
        TRUE ~ 0L
      ),
      phase_label = dplyr::case_when(
        direction_sign > 0 & amplitude_log_struct >=  major_move ~ "strong_offset",
        direction_sign > 0                                   ~ "weak_offset",
        direction_sign < 0 & abs(amplitude_log_struct) >= major_move ~ "strong_reversal",
        direction_sign < 0                                   ~ "weak_reversal",
        TRUE ~ "flat"
      )
    )
}

assign_swing_ids_to_years <- function(year_tbl, swing_tbl, swing_col = "swing_id") {
  year_tbl[[swing_col]] <- NA_integer_

  if (nrow(swing_tbl) == 0) return(year_tbl)

  for (j in seq_len(nrow(swing_tbl))) {
    y0 <- swing_tbl$start_year[j]
    y1 <- swing_tbl$end_year[j]

    idx <- if (j < nrow(swing_tbl)) {
      which(year_tbl$year >= y0 & year_tbl$year < y1)
    } else {
      which(year_tbl$year >= y0 & year_tbl$year <= y1)
    }

    year_tbl[[swing_col]][idx] <- swing_tbl$swing_id[j]
  }

  year_tbl
}

build_yearly_indices <- function(data, eps = 1e-10) {
  out <- data |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      d_pi = ln_pi_t - dplyr::lag(ln_pi_t),
      d_mu = ln_mu_t - dplyr::lag(ln_mu_t),
      d_p  = ln_p_t  - dplyr::lag(ln_p_t),
      d_B  = ln_B_t  - dplyr::lag(ln_B_t),
      d_nu = ln_nu_t - dplyr::lag(ln_nu_t),
      r_diag_t,
      r_struct_t,
      mu_t,
      theta_t,
      nu_level = nu_t - 1,
      chi_t,
      g_K_t,
      accounting_wedge_t
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      G_t = abs(d_pi) + abs(d_mu) + abs(d_p) + abs(d_B) + abs(d_nu),
      N_t = d_pi + d_mu + d_p + d_B + d_nu,
      D_t = dplyr::if_else(!is.na(G_t) & G_t > eps, 1 - abs(N_t) / G_t, NA_real_)
    )

  comp_mat <- as.matrix(out[, c("d_pi", "d_mu", "d_p", "d_B", "d_nu")])
  O_t <- rep(NA_real_, nrow(out))

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(out))) {
    Ni <- out$N_t[i]
    if (is.na(Ni)) next
    sgn <- sign_eps(Ni, eps = eps)
    if (sgn == 0L) {
      O_t[i] <- sum(abs(comp_mat[i, ]), na.rm = TRUE)
    } else {
      signs <- sign_eps(comp_mat[i, ], eps = eps)
      O_t[i] <- sum(abs(comp_mat[i, signs == -sgn]), na.rm = TRUE)
    }
  }

  out |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      O_t = O_t,
      S_off_t = dplyr::if_else(!is.na(G_t) & G_t > eps, O_t / G_t, NA_real_),
      F_rev_t = dplyr::if_else(!is.na(O_t) & !is.na(N_t) & (O_t + abs(N_t)) > eps, O_t / (O_t + abs(N_t)), NA_real_)
    )
}

# ── 3. Load and splice structural objects ────────────────────────────────────
stop_missing(path_stage1_master)
stop_missing(path_stage2_panel)
stop_missing(path_theta_isi)
stop_missing(path_theta_post)
stop_missing(path_capital_raw)
stop_missing(path_prices_raw)

stage1_master <- readRDS(path_stage1_master)
panel_stage2  <- readr::read_csv(path_stage2_panel, show_col_types = FALSE)
theta_isi     <- readr::read_csv(path_theta_isi, show_col_types = FALSE)
theta_post    <- readr::read_csv(path_theta_post, show_col_types = FALSE)

ect_isi  <- extract_stage1_ect(stage1_master, "ISI1931_1973")
ect_post <- extract_stage1_ect(stage1_master, "POST1974")

core <- panel_stage2 |>
  dplyr::select(year, y, k_nr, wsh) |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= 1932, year <= 2010)

isi_part <- theta_isi |>
  dplyr::select(year, regime_code, theta_r1, theta_r2, theta_active) |>
  dplyr::left_join(ect_isi, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::mutate(true_sample = "ISI1931_1973")

post_part <- theta_post |>
  dplyr::select(year, regime_code, theta_r1, theta_r2, theta_active) |>
  dplyr::left_join(ect_post, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::mutate(true_sample = "POST1974")

ts_splice <- dplyr::bind_rows(isi_part, post_part) |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= 1932, year <= 2010) |>
  dplyr::arrange(year) |>
  dplyr::left_join(core, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    regime_code = factor(regime_code, levels = c("low_ect_side", "high_ect_side")),
    dlog_k_nr = c(NA_real_, diff(k_nr))
  )

if (any(!is.finite(ts_splice$theta_active))) {
  stop("Spliced panel has missing theta_active values.", call. = FALSE)
}

ts_splice <- rescue_u_path(ts_splice, pinch_year = pinch_year)

# ── 4. Load Chile panel / raw sources ────────────────────────────────────────
c2_panel <- panel_stage2 |> janitor::clean_names()

if ("wsh" %in% names(c2_panel) && !("omega" %in% names(c2_panel))) {
  c2_panel$omega <- c2_panel$wsh
}
if (!("pi" %in% names(c2_panel)) && "wsh" %in% names(c2_panel)) {
  c2_panel$pi <- 1 - c2_panel$wsh
}

demand_raw <- tryCatch(
  readxl::read_excel(path_demand_raw) |> janitor::clean_names(),
  error = function(e) NULL
)

prices_raw <- readxl::read_excel(
  path_prices_raw,
  sheet = "4.1.3",
  skip = 9
) |>
  janitor::clean_names() |>
  dplyr::rename(
    year = code,
    pY   = defpgb,
    pC   = defc,
    pG   = defg,
    pK   = deffbkb,
    pX   = defx,
    pM   = defm
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(year, pY, pC, pG, pK, pX, pM)

tti_raw <- readxl::read_excel(
  path_prices_raw,
  sheet = "4.3.2",
  skip = 9
) |>
  janitor::clean_names() |>
  dplyr::rename(
    year = code,
    pTI = termint
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(year, pTI)

wp_raw <- readxl::read_excel(
  path_prices_raw,
  sheet = "4.4.1",
  skip = 9
) |>
  janitor::clean_names() |>
  dplyr::rename(
    year = code,
    wp = iwr
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(year, wp)

cpi_raw <- readxl::read_excel(
  path_prices_raw,
  sheet = "4.1.1",
  skip = 9
) |>
  janitor::clean_names() |>
  dplyr::rename(
    year = code,
    pCPI = ipc
  ) |>
  dplyr::select(year, pCPI)

prices_raw <- prices_raw |>
  dplyr::left_join(tti_raw, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::left_join(wp_raw, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::left_join(cpi_raw, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max)

required_price_cols <- c("year", "pY", "pK")
miss_price_cols <- required_price_cols[!required_price_cols %in% names(prices_raw)]
if (length(miss_price_cols) > 0) {
  stop(
    "prices_raw is missing required columns: ",
    paste(miss_price_cols, collapse = ", "),
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

price_tbl <- prices_raw |>
  dplyr::select(dplyr::any_of(c("year", "pY", "pC", "pG", "pK", "pX", "pM", "pTI", "wp", "pCPI"))) |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max)

capital_raw <- readr::read_csv(path_capital_raw, show_col_types = FALSE) |>
  janitor::clean_names()

# ── 5. Build merged Chile profitability panel ────────────────────────────────
base <- ts_splice |>
  dplyr::select(year, true_sample, regime_code, ect = ECT, theta_t = theta_active, y, y_p, mu_t, k_nr, wsh) |>
  dplyr::rename(omega_t = wsh)

acc <- c2_panel |>
  dplyr::select(dplyr::any_of(c(
    "year",
    "pi", "omega", "exploitation_rate",
    "gdp_real",
    "k_nr", "k_me", "k_total",
    "fbkf_me", "fbkf_nr", "i_total", "m_cif",
    "k_nr_gross", "k_total_gross", "k_gross",
    "k_net", "k_nr_net", "k_total_net"
  )))

if (!("k_gross" %in% names(acc))) {
  gross_hit <- intersect(c("k_total_gross", "k_nr_gross", "k_total", "k_nr"), names(acc))
  if (length(gross_hit) > 0) {
    acc <- dplyr::rename(acc, k_gross = !!rlang::sym(gross_hit[1]))
  }
}

if (!("k_net" %in% names(acc))) {
  net_hit <- intersect(c("k_total_net", "k_nr_net"), names(acc))
  if (length(net_hit) > 0) {
    acc <- dplyr::rename(acc, k_net = !!rlang::sym(net_hit[1]))
  } else if ("asset" %in% names(capital_raw) && "kn" %in% names(capital_raw)) {
    cap_net <- capital_raw |>
      dplyr::filter(.data$asset %in% c("Total", "NR", "K_Total", "K_NR")) |>
      dplyr::group_by(year) |>
      dplyr::summarise(k_net = dplyr::first(kn), .groups = "drop")
    acc <- acc |>
      dplyr::left_join(cap_net, by = "year")
  }
}

if (!("k_gross" %in% names(acc)) || all(is.na(acc$k_gross))) {
  if ("asset" %in% names(capital_raw) && "kg" %in% names(capital_raw)) {
    cap_gross <- capital_raw |>
      dplyr::filter(.data$asset %in% c("Total", "NR", "K_Total", "K_NR")) |>
      dplyr::group_by(year) |>
      dplyr::summarise(k_gross = dplyr::first(kg), .groups = "drop")
    acc <- acc |>
      dplyr::left_join(cap_gross, by = "year")
  }
}

if (!is.null(demand_raw)) {
  if (!("i_total" %in% names(acc))) {
    demand_i <- demand_raw |>
      rename_first(c("x1", "year", "anio", "ano"), "year", "demand year")
    it_col <- intersect(c("inversion_interna_bruta", "i_total", "fbkf_total"), names(demand_i))
    if (length(it_col) > 0) {
      acc <- acc |>
        dplyr::left_join(
          demand_i |>
            dplyr::select(year, i_total = !!rlang::sym(it_col[1])),
          by = "year"
        )
    }
  }

  if (!("gdp_real" %in% names(acc))) {
    demand_y <- demand_raw |>
      rename_first(c("x1", "year", "anio", "ano"), "year", "demand year")
    y_col <- intersect(c("pib_real_milllones_de_pesos_de_2003", "gdp_real", "y_real"), names(demand_y))
    if (length(y_col) > 0) {
      acc <- acc |>
        dplyr::left_join(
          demand_y |>
            dplyr::select(year, gdp_real = !!rlang::sym(y_col[1])),
          by = "year"
        )
    }
  }
}

d <- base |>
  dplyr::left_join(acc, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::left_join(price_tbl, by = "year") |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    omega_t = dplyr::coalesce(omega_t, omega),
    pi_t = dplyr::coalesce(pi, 1 - omega_t),

    GDP_real = dplyr::coalesce(gdp_real, exp(y)),
    Y_real   = exp(y),
    Yp_hat   = y_p,

    KGC = k_gross,
    KNC = k_net,

    pY_idx = pY,
    pK_idx = pK,
    pY_sc  = pY / 100,
    pK_sc  = pK / 100,

    GOS = pi_t * GDP_real * pY_sc,
    IGC = i_total * pK_sc
  )

required_now <- c(
  "year", "pi_t", "mu_t", "pY", "pK", "Yp_hat",
  "KGC", "KNC", "GOS", "IGC", "theta_t"
)

miss_now <- required_now[
  !required_now %in% names(d) |
    vapply(required_now, function(nm) all(is.na(d[[nm]])), logical(1))
]

if (length(miss_now) > 0) {
  stop(
    "Missing or unresolved Chile profitability inputs: ",
    paste(miss_now, collapse = ", "),
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

if (any(d$pi_t <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("pi_t has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$mu_t <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("mu_t has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$pY <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("pY has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$pK <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("pK has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$KGC <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("KGC has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$KNC <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("KNC has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)

# ── 6. Build structural profitability objects ────────────────────────────────
d <- d |>
  dplyr::arrange(year) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    p_t = pY / pK,
    B_t = Yp_hat / KGC,
    nu_t = KGC / KNC,

    r_struct_t    = pi_t * mu_t * p_t * B_t * nu_t,
    ln_r_struct_t = log(r_struct_t),

    r_diag_t    = GOS / KNC,
    ln_r_diag_t = log(r_diag_t),

    ln_pi_t = log(pi_t),
    ln_mu_t = log(mu_t),
    ln_p_t  = log(p_t),
    ln_B_t  = log(B_t),
    ln_nu_t = log(nu_t),

    ln_KNC_t = log(KNC),
    g_K_t    = ln_KNC_t - dplyr::lag(ln_KNC_t),

    chi_t = dplyr::if_else(!is.na(GOS) & abs(GOS) > 1e-8, IGC / GOS, NA_real_),

    accounting_wedge_t =
      dplyr::if_else(!is.na(r_diag_t) & abs(r_diag_t) > 1e-8, r_struct_t / r_diag_t, NA_real_)
  )

required_profitability <- c("r_struct_t", "r_diag_t", "p_t", "B_t", "nu_t", "chi_t")
miss_profitability <- required_profitability[
  !required_profitability %in% names(d) |
    vapply(required_profitability, function(nm) all(is.na(d[[nm]])), logical(1))
]

if (length(miss_profitability) > 0) {
  stop(
    "Profitability construction failed for: ",
    paste(miss_profitability, collapse = ", "),
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

if (any(d$r_struct_t <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("r_struct_t has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$r_diag_t <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("r_diag_t has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$nu_t < 1, na.rm = TRUE)) warning("nu_t < 1 detected; inspect gross/net stock consistency.", call. = FALSE)

# ── 7. Turning points and profit swings ──────────────────────────────────────
tp_raw <- find_turning_points_direction(
  year = d$year,
  x = d[[swing_xvar]],
  k = tp_k,
  span = tp_local_span
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_major <- prune_turning_points_windowed(
  tp = tp_raw,
  data = d,
  xvar = swing_xvar,
  break_year = tp_break_year,
  min_move_early = tp_min_move_early,
  min_years_early = tp_min_years_early,
  min_move_late = tp_min_move_late,
  min_years_late = tp_min_years_late
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_plot <- add_boundaries_for_plot(tp_major, d, swing_xvar) |>
  drop_weak_terminal_swing(
    data = d,
    xvar = swing_xvar,
    min_years = tp_terminal_min_years,
    min_move = tp_terminal_min_move
  )

# Major inferential swing table: no artificial boundaries
swing_tbl_major <- build_swing_table(tp_major, d) |>
  add_swing_decomposition(tp_major, d) |>
  add_swing_indices() |>
  classify_swing_phase(major_move = swing_major_move_cutoff)

# Plot swing table: includes artificial boundaries for coverage/figures only
swing_tbl_plot <- build_swing_table(tp_plot, d) |>
  add_swing_decomposition(tp_plot, d) |>
  add_swing_indices() |>
  classify_swing_phase(major_move = swing_major_move_cutoff)

tp_settings <- list(
  swing_xvar = swing_xvar,
  k = tp_k,
  local_span = tp_local_span,
  break_year = tp_break_year,
  min_move_early = tp_min_move_early,
  min_years_early = tp_min_years_early,
  min_move_late = tp_min_move_late,
  min_years_late = tp_min_years_late,
  terminal_min_move = tp_terminal_min_move,
  terminal_min_years = tp_terminal_min_years,
  swing_major_move_cutoff = swing_major_move_cutoff
)

tp_diagnostics <- list(
  raw = tp_raw,
  major = tp_major,
  plot = tp_plot,
  settings = tp_settings
)

# Keep backward compatibility for exporter while making semantics explicit
tp_env_final <- tp_plot

# ── 8. Yearly and swing recap/wedge objects ──────────────────────────────────
year_tbl_dys <- build_yearly_indices(d) |>
  assign_swing_ids_to_years(swing_tbl_major, swing_col = "swing_id_major") |>
  assign_swing_ids_to_years(swing_tbl_plot, swing_col = "swing_id_plot")

year_tbl_recap <- d |>
  dplyr::transmute(
    year,
    r_diag_t,
    g_K_t,
    chi_t,
    accounting_wedge_t,
    nu_level = nu_t - 1
  ) |>
  assign_swing_ids_to_years(swing_tbl_major, swing_col = "swing_id_major") |>
  assign_swing_ids_to_years(swing_tbl_plot, swing_col = "swing_id_plot")

swing_tbl_recap <- year_tbl_recap |>
  dplyr::filter(!is.na(swing_id_major)) |>
  dplyr::group_by(swing_id = swing_id_major) |>
  dplyr::summarise(
    avg_r_diag = mean(r_diag_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    avg_g_K = mean(g_K_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    avg_chi = mean(chi_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    chi_start = first_non_na(chi_t),
    chi_end   = last_non_na(chi_t),
    avg_accounting_wedge = mean(accounting_wedge_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    wedge_start = first_non_na(accounting_wedge_t),
    wedge_end   = last_non_na(accounting_wedge_t),
    avg_nu_level = mean(nu_level, na.rm = TRUE),
    .groups = "drop"
  ) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    delta_chi = chi_end - chi_start,
    delta_accounting_wedge = wedge_end - wedge_start
  )

swing_tbl_full <- swing_tbl_major |>
  dplyr::left_join(swing_tbl_recap, by = "swing_id")

# ── 9. Compact outputs ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
swing_tbl_compact <- swing_tbl_full |>
  dplyr::transmute(
    swing_id, start_year, end_year, direction, duration_years, phase_label,
    amplitude_pct_diag = round(amplitude_pct_diag, 1),
    amplitude_log_struct = round(amplitude_log_struct, 3),
    dist_share_pct = round(dist_share_pct, 1),
    util_share_pct = round(util_share_pct, 1),
    price_share_pct = round(price_share_pct, 1),
    capacity_share_pct = round(capacity_share_pct, 1),
    wedge_share_pct = round(wedge_share_pct, 1),
    G_swing = round(G_swing, 4),
    N_swing = round(N_swing, 4),
    D_swing = round(D_swing, 4),
    S_off_swing = round(S_off_swing, 4),
    F_rev_swing = round(F_rev_swing, 4),
    avg_chi = round(avg_chi, 4),
    avg_accounting_wedge = round(avg_accounting_wedge, 4)
  )

year_tbl_compact <- year_tbl_dys |>
  dplyr::transmute(
    year, swing_id_major, swing_id_plot,
    d_pi, d_mu, d_p, d_B, d_nu,
    G_t, N_t, D_t, S_off_t, F_rev_t,
    mu_t, theta_t, nu_level, chi_t, g_K_t
  )

accounting_wedge_summary <- d |>
  dplyr::summarise(
    mean_accounting_wedge = mean(accounting_wedge_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    sd_accounting_wedge   = sd(accounting_wedge_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    min_accounting_wedge  = min(accounting_wedge_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    max_accounting_wedge  = max(accounting_wedge_t, na.rm = TRUE),
    mean_nu_level         = mean(nu_t - 1, na.rm = TRUE),
    mean_chi              = mean(chi_t, na.rm = TRUE)
  )

analytical_bundle_chile <- list(
  d = d,

  swing_xvar = swing_xvar,
  tp_settings = tp_settings,
  tp_diagnostics = tp_diagnostics,

  tp_raw = tp_raw,
  tp_major = tp_major,
  tp_plot = tp_plot,
  tp_env_final = tp_env_final,   # backward-compatible alias for plotting/export

  swing_tbl_full = swing_tbl_full,   # inferential / major swings
  swing_tbl_major = swing_tbl_major,
  swing_tbl_plot = swing_tbl_plot,
  swing_tbl_compact = swing_tbl_compact,

  year_tbl_dys = year_tbl_dys,
  year_tbl_compact = year_tbl_compact,
  year_tbl_recap = year_tbl_recap,
  swing_tbl_recap = swing_tbl_recap,

  accounting_wedge_summary = accounting_wedge_summary
)

# ── 10. Save core objects ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
saveRDS(analytical_bundle_chile, file.path(rds_dir, "analytical_bundle_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(d, file.path(rds_dir, "d_merged_profitability_chile.rds"))

saveRDS(tp_raw, file.path(rds_dir, "tp_raw_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_major, file.path(rds_dir, "tp_major_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_plot, file.path(rds_dir, "tp_plot_chile.rds"))

saveRDS(swing_tbl_full, file.path(rds_dir, "swing_tbl_full_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(swing_tbl_major, file.path(rds_dir, "swing_tbl_major_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(swing_tbl_plot, file.path(rds_dir, "swing_tbl_plot_chile.rds"))

saveRDS(year_tbl_dys, file.path(rds_dir, "year_tbl_dys_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(year_tbl_recap, file.path(rds_dir, "year_tbl_recap_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(swing_tbl_recap, file.path(rds_dir, "swing_tbl_recap_chile.rds"))
saveRDS(accounting_wedge_summary, file.path(rds_dir, "accounting_wedge_summary_chile.rds"))

cat("Saved Chile profitability core objects to:\n")
cat("  ", rds_dir, "\n", sep = "")
cat("  analytical_bundle_chile.rds\n")
cat("  d_merged_profitability_chile.rds\n")
cat("  tp_raw_chile.rds\n")
cat("  tp_major_chile.rds\n")
cat("  tp_plot_chile.rds\n")

The key changes are: one swing carrier end-to-end (ln_r_struct_t), local-extremum dating, no duplicated break_year in windowed pruning, and a hard separation between tp_major for inference and tp_plot for figure coverage. Those are exactly the pressure points in your current builder. 

 


Next move should be the exporter harmonization pass so Figure 1 reads tp_plot, while comparative and interpretive tables read tp_major.

Check the difference of: fig01_profit_turning_points for the United States and fig01_chile_profitability_turning_points for the case of Chile, the algorithm looks both at the log difference of profitability smoothed, and the dynamics of the profit rate to develop an assesment of peak and through considering both, to report it after. Let's do the following workflow: 
- Creat a new code exclusively oriented to identify the profit swings and produce a CSV with the results based on the dynamics of: i) smoothed log-differential profitability, and ii) profit rate in level for a jointly peak to trough analysis.  ii) this code should note prune the window in the RHS of the time series out of the analysis also. 
- I'll run the code and we'll discuss the results, include a graphic visualization as the one for the US for the diagnostic, and set outputs to be delivered at "output/profitability_chile_diagnostic"

Thought for 2m 8s
Yes — the two figures are not methodologically aligned. The U.S. figure is a joint diagnostic: level profit rate plus smoothed Δ log(r). The Chile figure you showed is not doing that in a comparable way, so the safest move is a standalone diagnostic script that only does profit-swing identification and reporting. ⚙️

Use this as a new script, for example:

codes/01_chile_profit_swings_diagnostic.R

It writes everything to:

output/profitability_chile_diagnostic

and it does not prune the RHS terminal window out of the analysis.

###############################################################################
# CHILE — Profit swings diagnostic
# Standalone diagnostic script
#
# Purpose:
# - Identify Chile profit swings using a joint diagnostic:
#   (i) smoothed log-differential profitability
#   (ii) profit rate in level
# - Produce transparent CSV outputs for discussion
# - Produce a U.S.-style diagnostic figure:
#   solid line  = profit rate in level
#   dashed line = smoothed Δ log(profitability), secondary axis
#
# Key rules:
# - Detection is triggered by sign reversals in smoothed Δ log(r)
# - Dating is assigned to the local extremum of r in level
# - No RHS terminal window is dropped from the analysis
###############################################################################

# ── 0. Packages ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pkgs <- c("dplyr", "readr", "tibble", "zoo", "ggplot2", "janitor")
miss <- pkgs[!vapply(pkgs, requireNamespace, logical(1), quietly = TRUE)]
if (length(miss) > 0) install.packages(miss, repos = "https://cloud.r-project.org")
invisible(lapply(pkgs, library, character.only = TRUE))

# ── 1. Paths and controls ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
proj_root <- "C:/ReposGitHub/Capacity-Utilization-US_Chile"

# Prefer the merged profitability object from the Chile core if it exists
path_d_rds <- file.path(
  proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile", "rds", "d_merged_profitability_chile.rds"
)

# Fallback to bundle if needed
path_bundle_rds <- file.path(
  proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile", "rds", "analytical_bundle_chile.rds"
)

out_root <- file.path(proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile_diagnostic")
csv_dir  <- file.path(out_root, "csv")
fig_dir  <- file.path(out_root, "figures")
rds_dir  <- file.path(out_root, "rds")

dir.create(csv_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
dir.create(fig_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
dir.create(rds_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)

analysis_year_min <- 1940L
analysis_year_max <- 1978L

# Carrier settings
level_var <- "r_diag_t"      # level profit rate used for dating/reporting
log_var   <- "ln_r_diag_t"   # log profit rate used for Δlog signal

# Signal settings
k_smooth   <- 3L             # centered rolling mean for Δlog
local_span <- 1L             # local neighborhood around sign-change year

# Transparent pruning settings
# Note: these are light-touch diagnostic settings, and we DO NOT drop RHS terminal swing
min_years_between_tp <- 2L
min_log_move         <- 0.03

# Figure settings
fig_width  <- 12
fig_height <- 7
fig_dpi    <- 320

# ── 2. Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
stop_missing <- function(path) {
  if (!file.exists(path)) stop("Required file not found: ", path, call. = FALSE)
}

sign_eps <- function(x, eps = 1e-10) {
  ifelse(is.na(x) | abs(x) <= eps, 0L, ifelse(x > 0, 1L, -1L))
}

load_profitability_panel <- function(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds) {
  if (file.exists(path_d_rds)) {
    d <- readRDS(path_d_rds)
    return(d)
  }

  if (file.exists(path_bundle_rds)) {
    b <- readRDS(path_bundle_rds)
    if (!("d" %in% names(b))) stop("Bundle found, but object 'd' is missing.", call. = FALSE)
    return(b$d)
  }

  stop("Could not find either d_merged_profitability_chile.rds or analytical_bundle_chile.rds.", call. = FALSE)
}

locate_local_extremum <- function(year, level, i, type, span = 1L) {
  lo <- max(1L, i - span)
  hi <- min(length(level), i + span)
  win_idx <- lo:hi
  win_val <- level[win_idx]

  if (all(is.na(win_val))) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      idx = i,
      year = year[i],
      value = level[i],
      type = type
    ))
  }

  j <- if (type == "peak") {
    win_idx[which.max(win_val)]
  } else {
    win_idx[which.min(win_val)]
  }

  tibble::tibble(
    idx = j,
    year = year[j],
    value = level[j],
    type = type
  )
}

compute_signal_table <- function(df, level_var, log_var, k_smooth) {
  out <- df |>
    dplyr::arrange(year) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = .data[[level_var]],
      ln_r    = if (log_var %in% names(df)) .data[[log_var]] else log(.data[[level_var]])
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r = ln_r - dplyr::lag(ln_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed = zoo::rollmean(dlog_r, k = k_smooth, fill = NA, align = "center")
    )

  out
}

find_joint_turning_points <- function(signal_tbl, span = 1L, eps = 1e-10) {
  year  <- signal_tbl$year
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl$dlog_r_smoothed

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  if (length(sig) < 3) {
    return(tibble::tibble())
  }

  for (i in 2:(length(sig) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(sig[i - 1]) || is.na(sig[i])) next

    s_prev <- sign_eps(sig[i - 1], eps = eps)
    s_curr <- sign_eps(sig[i], eps = eps)

    if (s_prev > 0L && s_curr < 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, type = "peak", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    } else if (s_prev < 0L && s_curr > 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, type = "trough", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

compress_turning_points <- function(tp) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  keep <- vector("list", 0)
  current <- tp[1, , drop = FALSE]

  for (i in 2:nrow(tp)) {
    this <- tp[i, , drop = FALSE]

    if (this$type == current$type) {
      if (this$type == "peak" && this$value > current$value) current <- this
      if (this$type == "trough" && this$value < current$value) current <- this
    } else {
      keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
      current <- this
    }
  }

  keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
  dplyr::bind_rows(keep) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

prune_turning_points_joint <- function(tp, signal_tbl, min_years = 2L, min_log_move = 0.03) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  log_level <- log(level)
  out <- tp

  repeat {
    if (nrow(out) <= 1) break

    dur <- diff(out$year)
    amp_log <- abs(diff(log_level[out$idx]))
    weak <- which(dur < min_years | amp_log < min_log_move)

    if (length(weak) == 0) break

    k <- weak[1]

    if (k == 1) {
      out <- out[-2, , drop = FALSE]
    } else if (k == nrow(out) - 1) {
      out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
    } else {
      left_idx  <- out$idx[k - 1]
      a_idx     <- out$idx[k]
      b_idx     <- out$idx[k + 1]
      right_idx <- out$idx[k + 2]

      move_drop_left  <- abs(log_level[b_idx] - log_level[left_idx])
      move_drop_right <- abs(log_level[right_idx] - log_level[a_idx])

      if (move_drop_left >= move_drop_right) {
        out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
      } else {
        out <- out[-(k + 1), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }

    out <- compress_turning_points(out)
  }

  out
}

add_boundaries_keep_rhs <- function(tp, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp) == 0) {
    stop("No internal turning points detected. Try lowering smoothing/pruning thresholds.", call. = FALSE)
  }

  first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"

  start_row <- tibble::tibble(
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = 1L,
    year = signal_tbl$year[1],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[1],
    type = first_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  end_row <- tibble::tibble(
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = nrow(signal_tbl),
    year = signal_tbl$year[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    type = last_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  dplyr::bind_rows(start_row, tp, end_row) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

build_swing_table <- function(tp_bounds, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp_bounds) < 2) return(tibble::tibble())

  out <- vector("list", nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)) {
    idx0 <- tp_bounds$idx[i]
    idx1 <- tp_bounds$idx[i + 1]

    y0 <- tp_bounds$year[i]
    y1 <- tp_bounds$year[i + 1]

    r0 <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx0]
    r1 <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx1]

    ln0 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx0]
    ln1 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx1]

    dur <- y1 - y0

    out[[i]] <- tibble::tibble(
      swing_id = i,
      start_year = y0,
      end_year = y1,
      start_type = tp_bounds$type[i],
      end_type   = tp_bounds$type[i + 1],
      direction  = paste0(tp_bounds$type[i], "_to_", tp_bounds$type[i + 1]),
      duration_years = dur,
      start_r = r0,
      end_r   = r1,
      amplitude_pct = 100 * (r1 / r0 - 1),
      amplitude_log = ln1 - ln0,
      pace_pct_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, 100 * ((r1 / r0)^(1 / dur) - 1), NA_real_),
      pace_log_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, (ln1 - ln0) / dur, NA_real_),
      rhs_terminal_window = (i == (nrow(tp_bounds) - 1))
    )
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out)
}

plot_joint_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_final, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl$dlog_r_smoothed

  level_center <- mean(level, na.rm = TRUE)

  sig_range <- range(sig, na.rm = TRUE)
  lvl_range <- range(level, na.rm = TRUE)

  if (!all(is.finite(sig_range)) || diff(sig_range) == 0) {
    scale_fac <- 1
  } else {
    scale_fac <- 0.85 * diff(lvl_range) / diff(sig_range)
  }

  signal_tbl <- signal_tbl |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_plot = level_center + dlog_r_smoothed * scale_fac
    )

  tp_plot <- tp_final |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = value,
      type
    )

  p <- ggplot(signal_tbl, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = level_center, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = r_level), linewidth = 1.1) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_plot), linetype = "dashed", linewidth = 0.9) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "peak"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2,
      stroke = 0.8,
      fill = NA
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "trough"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2,
      stroke = 0.8,
      fill = NA
    ) +
    scale_shape_manual(values = c(peak = 24, trough = 25)) +
    scale_y_continuous(
      name = "profit rate",
      sec.axis = sec_axis(
        trans = ~ (. - level_center) / scale_fac,
        name = "smoothed Δ log profitability"
      )
    ) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      title = title_txt,
      shape = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, device = cairo_pdf)

  invisible(p)
}

# ── 3. Load data ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
d <- load_profitability_panel(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds)

required_vars <- c("year", level_var)
miss_vars <- required_vars[!required_vars %in% names(d)]
if (length(miss_vars) > 0) {
  stop("Missing required variable(s): ", paste(miss_vars, collapse = ", "), call. = FALSE)
}

d <- d |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max) |>
  dplyr::arrange(year)

if (!(log_var %in% names(d))) {
  d[[log_var]] <- log(d[[level_var]])
}

if (any(!is.finite(d[[level_var]]) | d[[level_var]] <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) {
  stop("Profit-rate level series contains non-positive or non-finite values.", call. = FALSE)
}

# ── 4. Compute signals ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
signal_tbl <- compute_signal_table(
  df = d,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth
)

# ── 5. Joint turning-point detection ─────────────────────────────────────────
tp_candidates <- find_joint_turning_points(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  span = local_span
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_final <- prune_turning_points_joint(
  tp = tp_candidates,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  min_years = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_bounds <- add_boundaries_keep_rhs(
  tp = tp_final,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

swings_tbl <- build_swing_table(
  tp_bounds = tp_bounds,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

# ── 6. Save outputs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
readr::write_csv(signal_tbl, file.path(csv_dir, "signal_table_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_candidates, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_candidates_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_final, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_final_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_bounds, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_with_boundaries_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(swings_tbl, file.path(csv_dir, "profit_swings_joint_diagnostic_chile.csv"))

saveRDS(signal_tbl, file.path(rds_dir, "signal_table_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_candidates, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_candidates_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_final, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_final_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_bounds, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_with_boundaries_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(swings_tbl, file.path(rds_dir, "profit_swings_joint_diagnostic_chile.rds"))

config_tbl <- tibble::tibble(
  analysis_year_min = analysis_year_min,
  analysis_year_max = analysis_year_max,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  local_span = local_span,
  min_years_between_tp = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move
)

readr::write_csv(config_tbl, file.path(csv_dir, "diagnostic_config_chile_profit_swings.csv"))

# ── 7. Figure ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  tp_final = tp_final,
  out_png = file.path(fig_dir, "fig01_chile_profit_turning_points_joint.png"),
  out_pdf = file.path(fig_dir, "fig01_chile_profit_turning_points_joint.pdf"),
  title_txt = NULL
)

A few important notes for this run. The script uses r_diag_t and ln_r_diag_t because your request is diagnostic and because the U.S. figure you referenced is built as a level-rate plus smoothed log-difference object. It also keeps the terminal sample window by construction, so the last swing remains visible instead of being quietly amputated.

turning_points_final_chile_profit_swings.csv,
profit_swings_joint_diagnostic_chile.csv,
and the new fig01_chile_profit_turning_points_joint.png. Then we can assess whether the sequence around 1971–1973 is reading historically as rebound → reversal → post-coup offset.

Thought for 1m 23s
Yes — and the run failure actually tells us something useful.

Right now the standalone diagnostic is doing what it was told to do: detect turning points from smoothed Δ log(r) and then prune them. In your run, that pruning stage eliminated all internal candidates, so add_boundaries_keep_rhs() hit an empty table and stopped with No internal turning points detected 


Also, the Chile core already carries ect into the merged analytical panel, so the diagnostic script can and should use it directly rather than reloading Stage 1 objects again. In the core, base is built with ect = ECT before merging into d 


The clean fix is:

keep turning-point detection driven by profitability

include ECT as a conditioning diagnostic, not as the trigger

make the script robust to prune-to-zero

export both the profitability swing tables and an ECT-aware diagnostic table/figure

Here is the patch set I would apply.

First, add these controls near the top of the standalone diagnostic script:

# Additional diagnostic controls
ect_var <- "ect"
ect_smooth_k <- 3L

# Fallback behavior:
# if pruning eliminates all internal TPs, keep the unpruned candidates for discussion
fallback_to_candidates_if_pruned_empty <- TRUE
Then replace compute_signal_table() with this version:

compute_signal_table <- function(df, level_var, log_var, k_smooth,
                                 ect_var = "ect", ect_smooth_k = 3L) {
  has_ect <- ect_var %in% names(df)

  out <- df |>
    dplyr::arrange(year) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = .data[[level_var]],
      ln_r    = if (log_var %in% names(df)) .data[[log_var]] else log(.data[[level_var]]),
      ect     = if (has_ect) .data[[ect_var]] else NA_real_
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r = ln_r - dplyr::lag(ln_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed = zoo::rollmean(dlog_r, k = k_smooth, fill = NA, align = "center"),
      ect_smoothed = if (has_ect) zoo::rollmean(ect, k = ect_smooth_k, fill = NA, align = "center") else NA_real_
    )

  zsafe <- function(x) {
    s <- stats::sd(x, na.rm = TRUE)
    m <- mean(x, na.rm = TRUE)
    if (!is.finite(s) || s <= 0) return(rep(NA_real_, length(x)))
    (x - m) / s
  }

  out |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r_smoothed_z = zsafe(dlog_r_smoothed),
      ect_z             = zsafe(ect),
      ect_smoothed_z    = zsafe(ect_smoothed)
    )
}
Then make the turning-point stage robust. Replace the current section from tp_candidates <- ... through tp_bounds <- ... with this:

tp_candidates <- find_joint_turning_points(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  span = local_span
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_final <- prune_turning_points_joint(
  tp = tp_candidates,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  min_years = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_status <- tibble::tibble(
  n_candidates = nrow(tp_candidates),
  n_after_prune = nrow(tp_final),
  used_fallback_candidates = FALSE
)

tp_for_analysis <- tp_final

if (nrow(tp_for_analysis) == 0 && fallback_to_candidates_if_pruned_empty && nrow(tp_candidates) > 0) {
  tp_for_analysis <- tp_candidates
  tp_status$used_fallback_candidates <- TRUE
}

if (nrow(tp_for_analysis) == 0) {
  stop(
    "No turning points survived detection. Inspect signal_tbl and lower smoothing or thresholds.",
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

tp_bounds <- add_boundaries_keep_rhs(
  tp = tp_for_analysis,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

swings_tbl <- build_swing_table(
  tp_bounds = tp_bounds,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)
That solves the immediate crash. Instead of dying when pruning wipes out the candidates, the script will transparently fall back to the detected candidates and record that in tp_status.

Now add an ECT-specific diagnostic figure. Keep the U.S.-style figure exactly as profitability-only, then create a second figure that shows whether turning points line up with external imbalance pressure.

Add this function:

plot_ect_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  p <- ggplot(signal_tbl, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_r_smoothed_z, linetype = "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_line(aes(y = ect_smoothed_z, linetype = "ECT external imbalance (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_vline(
      data = tp_used,
      aes(xintercept = year),
      linewidth = 0.35,
      alpha = 0.45
    ) +
    scale_linetype_manual(values = c(
      "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)" = "dashed",
      "ECT external imbalance (z)" = "solid"
    )) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      y = "standardized diagnostic scale",
      title = title_txt,
      linetype = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, device = cairo_pdf)

  invisible(p)
}

The substantive logic is this:

profitability still identifies the swing candidates

ECT tells you whether those candidates are occurring under growing or easing external disequilibrium

if pruning is too aggressive, the script no longer crashes; it reports that pruning wiped the set and uses candidates for discussion instead

That is the right diagnostic discipline for this stage. You want to inspect the object, not have the script pretend certainty by killing itself dramatically 😄
