Thought for 34s
Below is a single consolidated standalone diagnostic script. It patches the prune-to-zero failure you hit, and it includes ect explicitly in the diagnostic layer, using the merged Chile profitability panel where ect is already carried into d. 

 


###############################################################################
# CHILE — Profit swings diagnostic with ECT
# Standalone diagnostic script
#
# Purpose:
# - Identify Chile profit swings using a joint diagnostic:
#   (i) smoothed log-differential profitability
#   (ii) profit rate in level
# - Include ECT as a diagnostic layer for external imbalance pressure
# - Produce transparent CSV outputs for discussion
# - Produce a U.S.-style diagnostic figure:
#     solid line  = profit rate in level
#     dashed line = smoothed Δ log(profitability), secondary axis
# - Produce a second figure:
#     standardized smoothed Δ log(profitability) vs standardized ECT
#
# Key rules:
# - Detection is triggered by sign reversals in smoothed Δ log(r)
# - Dating is assigned to the local extremum of r in level
# - No RHS terminal window is dropped from the analysis
# - If pruning wipes out all internal turning points, fall back to candidates
###############################################################################

# ── 0. Packages ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
pkgs <- c("dplyr", "readr", "tibble", "zoo", "ggplot2", "janitor")
miss <- pkgs[!vapply(pkgs, requireNamespace, logical(1), quietly = TRUE)]
if (length(miss) > 0) install.packages(miss, repos = "https://cloud.r-project.org")
invisible(lapply(pkgs, library, character.only = TRUE))

# ── 1. Paths and controls ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
proj_root <- "C:/ReposGitHub/Capacity-Utilization-US_Chile"

path_d_rds <- file.path(
  proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile", "rds", "d_merged_profitability_chile.rds"
)

path_bundle_rds <- file.path(
  proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile", "rds", "analytical_bundle_chile.rds"
)

out_root <- file.path(proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile_diagnostic")
csv_dir  <- file.path(out_root, "csv")
fig_dir  <- file.path(out_root, "figures")
rds_dir  <- file.path(out_root, "rds")

dir.create(csv_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
dir.create(fig_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)
dir.create(rds_dir, recursive = TRUE, showWarnings = FALSE)

analysis_year_min <- 1940L
analysis_year_max <- 1978L

# Core carrier settings
level_var <- "r_diag_t"      # level profit rate used for dating/reporting
log_var   <- "ln_r_diag_t"   # log profit rate used for Δlog signal
ect_var   <- "ect"           # external disequilibrium / balance-of-payments diagnostic

# Signal settings
k_smooth     <- 3L           # centered rolling mean for Δlog
ect_smooth_k <- 3L           # centered rolling mean for ECT
local_span   <- 1L           # local neighborhood around sign-change year

# Transparent pruning settings
# NOTE: no RHS terminal swing is dropped
min_years_between_tp <- 2L
min_log_move         <- 0.03

# Fallback behavior if pruning wipes out all candidates
fallback_to_candidates_if_pruned_empty <- TRUE

# Figure settings
fig_width  <- 12
fig_height <- 7
fig_dpi    <- 320

# ── 2. Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
sign_eps <- function(x, eps = 1e-10) {
  ifelse(is.na(x) | abs(x) <= eps, 0L, ifelse(x > 0, 1L, -1L))
}

zsafe <- function(x) {
  s <- stats::sd(x, na.rm = TRUE)
  m <- mean(x, na.rm = TRUE)
  if (!is.finite(s) || s <= 0) return(rep(NA_real_, length(x)))
  (x - m) / s
}

load_profitability_panel <- function(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds) {
  if (file.exists(path_d_rds)) {
    d <- readRDS(path_d_rds)
    return(d)
  }

  if (file.exists(path_bundle_rds)) {
    b <- readRDS(path_bundle_rds)
    if (!("d" %in% names(b))) {
      stop("Bundle found, but object 'd' is missing.", call. = FALSE)
    }
    return(b$d)
  }

  stop(
    "Could not find either d_merged_profitability_chile.rds or analytical_bundle_chile.rds.",
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

locate_local_extremum <- function(year, level, i, type, span = 1L) {
  lo <- max(1L, i - span)
  hi <- min(length(level), i + span)
  win_idx <- lo:hi
  win_val <- level[win_idx]

  if (all(is.na(win_val))) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      idx = i,
      year = year[i],
      value = level[i],
      type = type
    ))
  }

  j <- if (type == "peak") {
    win_idx[which.max(win_val)]
  } else {
    win_idx[which.min(win_val)]
  }

  tibble::tibble(
    idx = j,
    year = year[j],
    value = level[j],
    type = type
  )
}

compute_signal_table <- function(df, level_var, log_var, k_smooth,
                                 ect_var = "ect", ect_smooth_k = 3L) {
  if (!(level_var %in% names(df))) {
    stop("Missing level_var in input data: ", level_var, call. = FALSE)
  }

  if (!(ect_var %in% names(df))) {
    stop("Missing ect_var in input data: ", ect_var, call. = FALSE)
  }

  out <- df |>
    dplyr::arrange(year) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = .data[[level_var]],
      ln_r    = if (log_var %in% names(df)) .data[[log_var]] else log(.data[[level_var]]),
      ect     = .data[[ect_var]]
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r = ln_r - dplyr::lag(ln_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed = zoo::rollmean(dlog_r, k = k_smooth, fill = NA, align = "center"),
      ect_smoothed    = zoo::rollmean(ect,    k = ect_smooth_k, fill = NA, align = "center")
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r_smoothed_z = zsafe(dlog_r_smoothed),
      ect_z             = zsafe(ect),
      ect_smoothed_z    = zsafe(ect_smoothed)
    )

  out
}

find_joint_turning_points <- function(signal_tbl, span = 1L, eps = 1e-10) {
  year  <- signal_tbl$year
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl$dlog_r_smoothed

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  if (length(sig) < 3) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  for (i in 2:(length(sig) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(sig[i - 1]) || is.na(sig[i])) next

    s_prev <- sign_eps(sig[i - 1], eps = eps)
    s_curr <- sign_eps(sig[i], eps = eps)

    if (s_prev > 0L && s_curr < 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, type = "peak", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    } else if (s_prev < 0L && s_curr > 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, type = "trough", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

compress_turning_points <- function(tp) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  keep <- vector("list", 0)
  current <- tp[1, , drop = FALSE]

  for (i in 2:nrow(tp)) {
    this <- tp[i, , drop = FALSE]

    if (this$type == current$type) {
      if (this$type == "peak"   && this$value > current$value) current <- this
      if (this$type == "trough" && this$value < current$value) current <- this
    } else {
      keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
      current <- this
    }
  }

  keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current

  dplyr::bind_rows(keep) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

prune_turning_points_joint <- function(tp, signal_tbl, min_years = 2L, min_log_move = 0.03) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  log_level <- log(level)
  out <- tp

  repeat {
    if (nrow(out) <= 1) break

    dur <- diff(out$year)
    amp_log <- abs(diff(log_level[out$idx]))
    weak <- which(dur < min_years | amp_log < min_log_move)

    if (length(weak) == 0) break

    k <- weak[1]

    if (k == 1) {
      out <- out[-2, , drop = FALSE]
    } else if (k == nrow(out) - 1) {
      out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
    } else {
      left_idx  <- out$idx[k - 1]
      a_idx     <- out$idx[k]
      b_idx     <- out$idx[k + 1]
      right_idx <- out$idx[k + 2]

      move_drop_left  <- abs(log_level[b_idx] - log_level[left_idx])
      move_drop_right <- abs(log_level[right_idx] - log_level[a_idx])

      if (move_drop_left >= move_drop_right) {
        out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
      } else {
        out <- out[-(k + 1), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }

    out <- compress_turning_points(out)
  }

  out
}

add_boundaries_keep_rhs <- function(tp, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp) == 0) {
    stop(
      "No internal turning points detected. Inspect signal table and thresholds.",
      call. = FALSE
    )
  }

  first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"

  start_row <- tibble::tibble(
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = 1L,
    year = signal_tbl$year[1],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[1],
    type = first_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  end_row <- tibble::tibble(
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = nrow(signal_tbl),
    year = signal_tbl$year[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    type = last_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  dplyr::bind_rows(start_row, tp, end_row) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

build_swing_table <- function(tp_bounds, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp_bounds) < 2) return(tibble::tibble())

  out <- vector("list", nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)) {
    idx0 <- tp_bounds$idx[i]
    idx1 <- tp_bounds$idx[i + 1]

    y0 <- tp_bounds$year[i]
    y1 <- tp_bounds$year[i + 1]

    r0  <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx0]
    r1  <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx1]
    ln0 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx0]
    ln1 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx1]

    ect0 <- signal_tbl$ect[idx0]
    ect1 <- signal_tbl$ect[idx1]
    ect_avg <- mean(signal_tbl$ect[idx0:idx1], na.rm = TRUE)
    ect_sm_avg <- mean(signal_tbl$ect_smoothed[idx0:idx1], na.rm = TRUE)

    dur <- y1 - y0

    out[[i]] <- tibble::tibble(
      swing_id = i,
      start_year = y0,
      end_year = y1,
      start_type = tp_bounds$type[i],
      end_type   = tp_bounds$type[i + 1],
      direction  = paste0(tp_bounds$type[i], "_to_", tp_bounds$type[i + 1]),
      duration_years = dur,
      start_r = r0,
      end_r   = r1,
      amplitude_pct = 100 * (r1 / r0 - 1),
      amplitude_log = ln1 - ln0,
      pace_pct_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, 100 * ((r1 / r0)^(1 / dur) - 1), NA_real_),
      pace_log_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, (ln1 - ln0) / dur, NA_real_),
      ect_start = ect0,
      ect_end   = ect1,
      ect_avg   = ect_avg,
      ect_smoothed_avg = ect_sm_avg,
      rhs_terminal_window = (i == (nrow(tp_bounds) - 1))
    )
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out)
}

plot_joint_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl$dlog_r_smoothed

  level_center <- mean(level, na.rm = TRUE)
  sig_range <- range(sig, na.rm = TRUE)
  lvl_range <- range(level, na.rm = TRUE)

  if (!all(is.finite(sig_range)) || diff(sig_range) == 0) {
    scale_fac <- 1
  } else {
    scale_fac <- 0.85 * diff(lvl_range) / diff(sig_range)
  }

  signal_plot <- signal_tbl |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_plot = level_center + dlog_r_smoothed * scale_fac
    )

  tp_plot <- tp_used |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = value,
      type
    )

  p <- ggplot(signal_plot, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = level_center, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = r_level), linewidth = 1.1) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_plot), linetype = "dashed", linewidth = 0.9) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "peak"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2, stroke = 0.8, fill = NA
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "trough"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2, stroke = 0.8, fill = NA
    ) +
    scale_shape_manual(values = c(peak = 24, trough = 25)) +
    scale_y_continuous(
      name = "profit rate",
      sec.axis = sec_axis(
        trans = ~ (. - level_center) / scale_fac,
        name = "smoothed Δ log profitability"
      )
    ) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      title = title_txt,
      shape = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height)

  invisible(p)
}

plot_ect_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  p <- ggplot(signal_tbl, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_r_smoothed_z, linetype = "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_line(aes(y = ect_smoothed_z, linetype = "ECT external imbalance (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_vline(
      data = tp_used,
      aes(xintercept = year),
      linewidth = 0.35,
      alpha = 0.45
    ) +
    scale_linetype_manual(values = c(
      "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)" = "dashed",
      "ECT external imbalance (z)" = "solid"
    )) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      y = "standardized diagnostic scale",
      title = title_txt,
      linetype = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height)

  invisible(p)
}

# ── 3. Load data ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
d <- load_profitability_panel(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds)

required_vars <- c("year", level_var, ect_var)
miss_vars <- required_vars[!required_vars %in% names(d)]
if (length(miss_vars) > 0) {
  stop("Missing required variable(s): ", paste(miss_vars, collapse = ", "), call. = FALSE)
}

d <- d |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max) |>
  dplyr::arrange(year)

if (!(log_var %in% names(d))) {
  d[[log_var]] <- log(d[[level_var]])
}

if (any(!is.finite(d[[level_var]]) | d[[level_var]] <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) {
  stop("Profit-rate level series contains non-positive or non-finite values.", call. = FALSE)
}

# ── 4. Compute signals ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
signal_tbl <- compute_signal_table(
  df = d,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  ect_smooth_k = ect_smooth_k
)

# ── 5. Joint turning-point detection ─────────────────────────────────────────
tp_candidates <- find_joint_turning_points(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  span = local_span
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_final_pruned <- prune_turning_points_joint(
  tp = tp_candidates,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  min_years = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_status <- tibble::tibble(
  n_candidates = nrow(tp_candidates),
  n_after_prune = nrow(tp_final_pruned),
  used_fallback_candidates = FALSE
)

tp_used <- tp_final_pruned

if (nrow(tp_used) == 0 && fallback_to_candidates_if_pruned_empty && nrow(tp_candidates) > 0) {
  tp_used <- tp_candidates
  tp_status$used_fallback_candidates <- TRUE
}

if (nrow(tp_used) == 0) {
  stop(
    "No turning points survived detection. Inspect signal_tbl and lower smoothing or thresholds.",
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

tp_bounds <- add_boundaries_keep_rhs(
  tp = tp_used,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

swings_tbl <- build_swing_table(
  tp_bounds = tp_bounds,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

config_tbl <- tibble::tibble(
  analysis_year_min = analysis_year_min,
  analysis_year_max = analysis_year_max,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  ect_smooth_k = ect_smooth_k,
  local_span = local_span,
  min_years_between_tp = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move,
  fallback_to_candidates_if_pruned_empty = fallback_to_candidates_if_pruned_empty
)

# ── 6. Save outputs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
readr::write_csv(config_tbl, file.path(csv_dir, "diagnostic_config_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_status, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_status_chile_profit_swings.csv"))

readr::write_csv(signal_tbl, file.path(csv_dir, "signal_table_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_candidates, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_candidates_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_final_pruned, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_final_pruned_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_used, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_used_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(tp_bounds, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_with_boundaries_chile_profit_swings.csv"))
readr::write_csv(swings_tbl, file.path(csv_dir, "profit_swings_joint_diagnostic_chile.csv"))

saveRDS(config_tbl, file.path(rds_dir, "diagnostic_config_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_status, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_status_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(signal_tbl, file.path(rds_dir, "signal_table_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_candidates, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_candidates_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_final_pruned, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_final_pruned_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_used, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_used_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(tp_bounds, file.path(rds_dir, "turning_points_with_boundaries_chile_profit_swings.rds"))
saveRDS(swings_tbl, file.path(rds_dir, "profit_swings_joint_diagnostic_chile.rds"))

What changed is straightforward: the script now includes ect in the signal table and in the swing summary, and it no longer dies just because pruning erased all internal turning points; it records that outcome and falls back to the detected candidates for discussion. That directly addresses the failure you showed. 



Error: No turning points survived detection. Inspect signal_tbl and lower smoothing or thresholds.

Thought for 1m 14s
That error means the script found no internal sign reversals in the profitability signal that survived detection. In practice, that usually means one of two things: either the Chile diagnostic rate is too monotone under the current carrier, or the smoothing/detection rule is too strict for this sample.

So the right fix is not to make the script die. The right fix is to make it:

try the primary rule first,

fall back to weaker diagnostic rules if needed,

always export what happened,

and include ECT as a parallel structural-imbalance diagnostic.

Use this fully patched standalone script. It writes to output/profitability_chile_diagnostic, includes ECT, and it will not crash when internal turning points are absent.

###############################################################################
# CHILE — Profit swings diagnostic with ECT
# Standalone diagnostic script
#
# Purpose:
# - Identify Chile profit swings using a joint diagnostic:
#   (i) smoothed log-differential profitability
#   (ii) profit rate in level
# - Include ECT as a diagnostic layer for external imbalance pressure
# - Produce transparent CSV outputs for discussion
# - Produce a U.S.-style diagnostic figure:
#     solid line  = profit rate in level
#     dashed line = smoothed Δ log(profitability), secondary axis
# - Produce a second figure:
#     standardized smoothed Δ log(profitability) vs standardized ECT
#
# Detection ladder:
# - primary: sign reversals in smoothed Δlog(r)
# - fallback 1: sign reversals in raw Δlog(r)
# - fallback 2: local extrema in profit-rate levels
#
# Key rules:
# - dating is assigned to local extrema of the profit-rate level
# - RHS terminal window is NOT dropped
# - if no internal turning points exist, the script still exports diagnostics
###############################################################################

# ── 0. Packages ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

miss <- pkgs[!vapply(pkgs, requireNamespace, logical(1), quietly = TRUE)]
if (length(miss) > 0) install.packages(miss, repos = "https://cloud.r-project.org")
invisible(lapply(pkgs, library, character.only = TRUE))

# ── 1. Paths and controls ────────────────────────────────────────────────────
proj_root <- "C:/ReposGitHub/Capacity-Utilization-US_Chile"

path_d_rds <- file.path(
  proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile", "rds", "d_merged_profitability_chile.rds"
)

  proj_root, "output", "profitability_chile", "rds", "analytical_bundle_chile.rds"

# Carrier settings

# ── 2. Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
sign_eps <- function(x, eps = 1e-10) {
  ifelse(is.na(x) | abs(x) <= eps, 0L, ifelse(x > 0, 1L, -1L))
}

zsafe <- function(x) {
  s <- stats::sd(x, na.rm = TRUE)
  m <- mean(x, na.rm = TRUE)
  if (!is.finite(s) || s <= 0) return(rep(NA_real_, length(x)))
  (x - m) / s
}

load_profitability_panel <- function(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds) {
  if (file.exists(path_d_rds)) {
    return(readRDS(path_d_rds))
  }

  if (file.exists(path_bundle_rds)) {
    b <- readRDS(path_bundle_rds)
    if (!("d" %in% names(b))) {
      stop("Bundle found, but object 'd' is missing.", call. = FALSE)
    }
    return(b$d)
  }

  stop(
    "Could not find either d_merged_profitability_chile.rds or analytical_bundle_chile.rds.",
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

locate_local_extremum <- function(year, level, i, type, span = 1L) {
  lo <- max(1L, i - span)
  hi <- min(length(level), i + span)
  win_idx <- lo:hi
  win_val <- level[win_idx]

  if (all(is.na(win_val))) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      idx = i,
      year = year[i],
      value = level[i],
      type = type
    ))
  }

  j <- if (type == "peak") {
    win_idx[which.max(win_val)]
  } else {
    win_idx[which.min(win_val)]
  }

  tibble::tibble(
    idx = j,
    year = year[j],
    value = level[j],
    type = type
  )
}

compute_signal_table <- function(df, level_var, log_var, k_smooth,
                                 ect_var = "ect", ect_smooth_k = 3L) {
  if (!(level_var %in% names(df))) {
    stop("Missing level_var in input data: ", level_var, call. = FALSE)
  }
  if (!(ect_var %in% names(df))) {
    stop("Missing ect_var in input data: ", ect_var, call. = FALSE)
  }

  out <- df |>
    dplyr::arrange(year) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = .data[[level_var]],
      ln_r    = if (log_var %in% names(df)) .data[[log_var]] else log(.data[[level_var]]),
      ect     = .data[[ect_var]]
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r = ln_r - dplyr::lag(ln_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed = zoo::rollmean(dlog_r, k = k_smooth, fill = NA, align = "center"),
      ect_smoothed    = zoo::rollmean(ect, k = ect_smooth_k, fill = NA, align = "center")
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r_z          = zsafe(dlog_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed_z = zsafe(dlog_r_smoothed),
      ect_z             = zsafe(ect),
      ect_smoothed_z    = zsafe(ect_smoothed)
    )

  out
}

compress_turning_points <- function(tp) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  keep <- vector("list", 0)
  current <- tp[1, , drop = FALSE]

  for (i in 2:nrow(tp)) {
    this <- tp[i, , drop = FALSE]

    if (this$type == current$type) {
      if (this$type == "peak"   && this$value > current$value) current <- this
      if (this$type == "trough" && this$value < current$value) current <- this
    } else {
      keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
      current <- this
    }
  }

  keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
  dplyr::bind_rows(keep) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

find_tp_from_signal <- function(signal_tbl, signal_col, span = 1L, eps = 1e-10, method_name = "signal_rule") {
  year  <- signal_tbl$year
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl[[signal_col]]

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  if (length(sig) < 3) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  for (i in 2:(length(sig) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(sig[i - 1]) || is.na(sig[i])) next

    s_prev <- sign_eps(sig[i - 1], eps = eps)
    s_curr <- sign_eps(sig[i], eps = eps)

    if (s_prev > 0L && s_curr < 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "peak", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = method_name,
        signal_col = signal_col,
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    } else if (s_prev < 0L && s_curr > 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "trough", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = method_name,
        signal_col = signal_col,
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

find_tp_from_levels <- function(signal_tbl, span = 1L) {
  year  <- signal_tbl$year
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  if (length(level) < 3) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  for (i in 2:(length(level) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(level[i - 1]) || is.na(level[i]) || is.na(level[i + 1])) next

    if (level[i - 1] < level[i] && level[i] > level[i + 1]) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "peak", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = "level_extrema",
        signal_col = "r_level",
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = NA_real_,
        signal_curr = NA_real_,
        signal_strength = NA_real_
      )
    } else if (level[i - 1] > level[i] && level[i] < level[i + 1]) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "trough", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = "level_extrema",
        signal_col = "r_level",
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = NA_real_,
        signal_curr = NA_real_,
        signal_strength = NA_real_
      )
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

prune_turning_points_joint <- function(tp, signal_tbl, min_years = 2L, min_log_move = 0.03) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  log_level <- log(level)
  out <- tp

  repeat {
    if (nrow(out) <= 1) break

    dur <- diff(out$year)
    amp_log <- abs(diff(log_level[out$idx]))
    weak <- which(dur < min_years | amp_log < min_log_move)

    if (length(weak) == 0) break

    k <- weak[1]

    if (k == 1) {
      out <- out[-2, , drop = FALSE]
    } else if (k == nrow(out) - 1) {
      out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
    } else {
      left_idx  <- out$idx[k - 1]
      a_idx     <- out$idx[k]
      b_idx     <- out$idx[k + 1]
      right_idx <- out$idx[k + 2]

      move_drop_left  <- abs(log_level[b_idx] - log_level[left_idx])
      move_drop_right <- abs(log_level[right_idx] - log_level[a_idx])

      if (move_drop_left >= move_drop_right) {
        out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
      } else {
        out <- out[-(k + 1), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }

    out <- compress_turning_points(out)
  }

  out
}

make_boundary_only_tp <- function(signal_tbl) {
  level_first <- signal_tbl$r_level[1]
  level_last  <- signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)]

  start_type <- if (level_last >= level_first) "trough" else "peak"
  end_type   <- if (start_type == "trough") "peak" else "trough"

  tibble::tibble(
    method = "boundary_only",
    signal_col = NA_character_,
    signal_idx = c(NA_integer_, NA_integer_),
    signal_year = c(NA_integer_, NA_integer_),
    idx = c(1L, nrow(signal_tbl)),
    year = c(signal_tbl$year[1], signal_tbl$year[nrow(signal_tbl)]),
    value = c(signal_tbl$r_level[1], signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)]),
    type = c(start_type, end_type),
    signal_prev = c(NA_real_, NA_real_),
    signal_curr = c(NA_real_, NA_real_),
    signal_strength = c(NA_real_, NA_real_)
  )
}

add_boundaries_keep_rhs <- function(tp, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp) == 0) {
    return(make_boundary_only_tp(signal_tbl))
  }

  first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"

  start_row <- tibble::tibble(
    method = "boundary",
    signal_col = NA_character_,
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = 1L,
    year = signal_tbl$year[1],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[1],
    type = first_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  end_row <- tibble::tibble(
    method = "boundary",
    signal_col = NA_character_,
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = nrow(signal_tbl),
    year = signal_tbl$year[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    type = last_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  dplyr::bind_rows(start_row, tp, end_row) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

build_swing_table <- function(tp_bounds, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp_bounds) < 2) return(tibble::tibble())

  out <- vector("list", nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)) {
    idx0 <- tp_bounds$idx[i]
    idx1 <- tp_bounds$idx[i + 1]

    y0 <- tp_bounds$year[i]
    y1 <- tp_bounds$year[i + 1]

    r0  <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx0]
    r1  <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx1]
    ln0 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx0]
    ln1 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx1]

    ect0 <- signal_tbl$ect[idx0]
    ect1 <- signal_tbl$ect[idx1]
    ect_avg <- mean(signal_tbl$ect[idx0:idx1], na.rm = TRUE)
    ect_sm_avg <- mean(signal_tbl$ect_smoothed[idx0:idx1], na.rm = TRUE)

    dur <- y1 - y0

    out[[i]] <- tibble::tibble(
      swing_id = i,
      start_year = y0,
      end_year = y1,
      start_type = tp_bounds$type[i],
      end_type   = tp_bounds$type[i + 1],
      direction  = paste0(tp_bounds$type[i], "_to_", tp_bounds$type[i + 1]),
      duration_years = dur,
      start_r = r0,
      end_r   = r1,
      amplitude_pct = 100 * (r1 / r0 - 1),
      amplitude_log = ln1 - ln0,
      pace_pct_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, 100 * ((r1 / r0)^(1 / dur) - 1), NA_real_),
      pace_log_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, (ln1 - ln0) / dur, NA_real_),
      ect_start = ect0,
      ect_end   = ect1,
      ect_avg   = ect_avg,
      ect_smoothed_avg = ect_sm_avg,
      boundary_only = all(tp_bounds$method == "boundary_only"),
      rhs_terminal_window = (i == (nrow(tp_bounds) - 1))
    )
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out)
}

plot_joint_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl$dlog_r_smoothed

  level_center <- mean(level, na.rm = TRUE)
  sig_range <- range(sig, na.rm = TRUE)
  lvl_range <- range(level, na.rm = TRUE)

  if (!all(is.finite(sig_range)) || diff(sig_range) == 0) {
    scale_fac <- 1
  } else {
    scale_fac <- 0.85 * diff(lvl_range) / diff(sig_range)
  }

  signal_plot <- signal_tbl |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_plot = level_center + dlog_r_smoothed * scale_fac
    )

  tp_plot <- tp_used |>
    dplyr::filter(!method %in% c("boundary", "boundary_only")) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = value,
      type
    )

  p <- ggplot(signal_plot, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = level_center, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = r_level), linewidth = 1.1) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_plot), linetype = "dashed", linewidth = 0.9) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "peak"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2, stroke = 0.8, fill = NA
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "trough"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2, stroke = 0.8, fill = NA
    ) +
    scale_shape_manual(values = c(peak = 24, trough = 25)) +
    scale_y_continuous(
      name = "profit rate",
      sec.axis = sec_axis(
        trans = ~ (. - level_center) / scale_fac,
        name = "smoothed Δ log profitability"
      )
    ) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      title = title_txt,
      shape = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height)

  invisible(p)
}

plot_ect_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  tp_vlines <- tp_used |>
    dplyr::filter(!method %in% c("boundary", "boundary_only"))

  p <- ggplot(signal_tbl, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_r_smoothed_z, linetype = "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_line(aes(y = ect_smoothed_z, linetype = "ECT external imbalance (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_vline(
      data = tp_vlines,
      aes(xintercept = year),
      linewidth = 0.35,
      alpha = 0.45
    ) +
    scale_linetype_manual(values = c(
      "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)" = "dashed",
      "ECT external imbalance (z)" = "solid"
    )) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      y = "standardized diagnostic scale",
      title = title_txt,
      linetype = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height)

  invisible(p)
}

# ── 3. Load data ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
d <- load_profitability_panel(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds)

required_vars <- c("year", level_var, ect_var)
miss_vars <- required_vars[!required_vars %in% names(d)]
if (length(miss_vars) > 0) {
  stop("Missing required variable(s): ", paste(miss_vars, collapse = ", "), call. = FALSE)
}

d <- d |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max) |>
  dplyr::arrange(year)

if (!(log_var %in% names(d))) {
  d[[log_var]] <- log(d[[level_var]])
}

if (any(!is.finite(d[[level_var]]) | d[[level_var]] <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) {
  stop("Profit-rate level series contains non-positive or non-finite values.", call. = FALSE)
}

# ── 4. Compute signals ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
signal_tbl <- compute_signal_table(
  df = d,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  ect_smooth_k = ect_smooth_k
)

# ── 5. Detection ladder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
tp_candidates_primary <- find_tp_from_signal(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  signal_col = "dlog_r_smoothed",
  span = local_span,
  method_name = "smoothed_dlog_rule"
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_candidates_raw <- find_tp_from_signal(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  signal_col = "dlog_r",
  span = local_span,
  method_name = "raw_dlog_rule"
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_candidates_level <- find_tp_from_levels(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  span = local_span
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_candidates_used <- tp_candidates_primary
candidate_method_used <- "smoothed_dlog_rule"

if (nrow(tp_candidates_used) == 0 && nrow(tp_candidates_raw) > 0) {
  tp_candidates_used <- tp_candidates_raw
  candidate_method_used <- "raw_dlog_rule"
}

if (nrow(tp_candidates_used) == 0 && nrow(tp_candidates_level) > 0) {
  tp_candidates_used <- tp_candidates_level
  candidate_method_used <- "level_extrema"
}

tp_final_pruned <- if (nrow(tp_candidates_used) > 0) {
  prune_turning_points_joint(
    tp = tp_candidates_used,
    signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
    min_years = min_years_between_tp,
    min_log_move = min_log_move
  ) |>
    compress_turning_points()
} else {
  tp_candidates_used
}

tp_used <- tp_final_pruned
used_boundary_only <- FALSE

if (nrow(tp_used) == 0) {
  tp_used <- make_boundary_only_tp(signal_tbl)
  used_boundary_only <- TRUE
}

tp_bounds <- if (used_boundary_only) {
  tp_used
} else {
  add_boundaries_keep_rhs(
    tp = tp_used,
    signal_tbl = signal_tbl
  )
}

swings_tbl <- build_swing_table(
  tp_bounds = tp_bounds,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

tp_status <- tibble::tibble(
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  n_candidates_primary = nrow(tp_candidates_primary),
  n_candidates_raw = nrow(tp_candidates_raw),
  n_candidates_level = nrow(tp_candidates_level),
  candidate_method_used = candidate_method_used,
  n_candidates_used = nrow(tp_candidates_used),
  n_after_prune = nrow(tp_final_pruned),
  used_boundary_only = used_boundary_only
)

config_tbl <- tibble::tibble(
  analysis_year_min = analysis_year_min,
  analysis_year_max = analysis_year_max,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  ect_smooth_k = ect_smooth_k,
  local_span = local_span,
  min_years_between_tp = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move
)

readr::write_csv(tp_status, file.path(csv_dir, "turning_points_status_chile_profit_swings.csv"))

analyze, why there is a flat dynamics, I think we have problems of scale in the determination of the profit rate, so we'll need to audit as well the order of magnitud of building varaibles 

Thought for 2m 54s
Yes — the “flat” line is not mainly a turning-point problem. It is a measurement-scale problem in r_diag_t. ⚠️

What the diagnostic is showing is this: the plotted profit rate is microscopic for most of the sample and then explodes late. In the CSV you uploaded, r_level goes from about 3.38e-10 in 1940 to 3.94e-03 in 1978. So the series is not truly flat; it is compressed near zero for decades because its order of magnitude is wrong, then it lifts abruptly when the price component starts dominating.

The core reason is in the builder. Right now you define:

GOS = pi_t * GDP_real * pY_sc
KNC = k_net
r_diag_t = GOS / KNC
But GOS is being converted into current-price terms using pY_sc, while KNC is left unrevalued. There is no corresponding KNC_nom = KNC * pK_sc before forming r_diag_t. So the numerator is current-price, the denominator is still effectively constant-price/base-price. That makes early years collapse toward zero and later years rise mechanically with the price level. 


That also explains why the primary smoothed-Δlog rule found no candidates and the script had to fall back: the smoothed signal sees a mostly monotone upward drift, not a meaningful cyclical profitability pattern. The earlier crash you got was already hinting that the detected signal structure was too thin after pruning. 


So the first diagnosis is:

the flat Chile diagnostic figure is mostly a numeraire inconsistency, not an absence of dynamics.

The second diagnosis is:

there may also be a plain unit mismatch on top of that — for example, GDP_real might be in millions while KNC is in pesos, or vice versa. If that is happening, even repricing the denominator will not fully fix the order of magnitude.

The right audit is to compare three candidate rates side by side:

# Run this on d_merged_profitability_chile.rds after loading object d

audit_df <- d |>
  dplyr::transmute(
    year,
    pi_t,
    GDP_real,
    pY_sc,
    pK_sc,
    GOS_current = GOS,
    KNC_real = KNC,
    KGC_real = KGC,

    # current-price repricing of the denominator
    KNC_current = KNC * pK_sc,
    KGC_current = KGC * pK_sc,

    # currently used diagnostic rate
    r_diag_current_mixed = r_diag_t,

    # candidate 1: fully real
    r_diag_real_net  = (pi_t * GDP_real) / KNC,
    r_diag_real_gross = (pi_t * GDP_real) / KGC,

    # candidate 2: fully current-price
    r_diag_current_net  = GOS / (KNC * pK_sc),
    r_diag_current_gross = GOS / (KGC * pK_sc),

    # logs for scale audit
    log10_GDP_real    = log10(abs(GDP_real)),
    log10_GOS_current = log10(abs(GOS)),
    log10_KNC_real    = log10(abs(KNC)),
    log10_KNC_current = log10(abs(KNC * pK_sc))
  )

summary_tbl <- audit_df |>
  dplyr::summarise(
    dplyr::across(
      c(GDP_real, GOS_current, KNC_real, KNC_current,
        r_diag_current_mixed, r_diag_real_net, r_diag_current_net),
      list(min = ~min(., na.rm = TRUE),
           median = ~median(., na.rm = TRUE),
           max = ~max(., na.rm = TRUE))
    )
  )

period_tbl <- audit_df |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    period = dplyr::case_when(
      year <= 1952 ~ "1940-1952",
      year <= 1964 ~ "1953-1964",
      year <= 1973 ~ "1965-1973",
      TRUE         ~ "1974-1978"
    )
  ) |>
  dplyr::group_by(period) |>
  dplyr::summarise(
    med_r_diag_current_mixed = median(r_diag_current_mixed, na.rm = TRUE),
    med_r_diag_real_net      = median(r_diag_real_net, na.rm = TRUE),
    med_r_diag_current_net   = median(r_diag_current_net, na.rm = TRUE),
    med_log10_GOS_current    = median(log10_GOS_current, na.rm = TRUE),
    med_log10_KNC_real       = median(log10_KNC_real, na.rm = TRUE),
    med_log10_KNC_current    = median(log10_KNC_current, na.rm = TRUE),
    .groups = "drop"
  )

print(summary_tbl)
print(period_tbl)
What I expect from that audit is:

r_diag_current_mixed will look absurdly tiny early and trend upward almost mechanically.

r_diag_current_net = GOS / (KNC * pK_sc) should be much more plausible.

If r_diag_current_net is still absurd, then the remaining problem is units between GDP_real and KNC.

The practical repair path is:

First, freeze the diagnosis that the current r_diag_t is not admissible for swing identification.

Second, rebuild the diagnostic rate as one of these two coherent objects:
r_diag_real = (pi_t * GDP_real) / KNC if both are in the same real units, or
r_diag_current = GOS / (KNC * pK_sc) if you want a current-price rate.

Third, rerun the standalone turning-point diagnostic on the repaired rate, not on the current mixed one.

The key punchline is simple: the Chile figure looks flat because the code is currently dividing a repriced numerator by an unrepriced denominator. That is exactly the kind of scale bug that makes a time series look dead for thirty years and then suddenly “come alive.” A very theatrical bug, but still a bug 😄

Paste the output of that audit table and we can decide immediately whether the main issue is asymmetric repricing only, or asymmetric repricing plus a deeper units mismatch.

Thought for 33s
Perfect. This audit basically convicts the current r_diag_t on the spot 🔍

The key result is here:

med_r_diag_current_mixed:

1940–1952: 8.73e-10

1953–1964: 3.74e-08

1965–1973: 5.89e-07

1974–1978: 1.56e-03

versus

med_r_diag_real_net:

1940–1952: 0.0924

1953–1964: 0.110

1965–1973: 0.109

1974–1978: 0.103

That means the apparent “flatness” is not a lack of profit-rate dynamics. It is a scale pathology from the mixed diagnostic rate.

So the diagnosis is now very strong:

The current r_diag_t = GOS / KNC is dimensionally inconsistent because GOS was repriced while KNC was not.

The resulting series is crushed near zero for most of the sample.

The turning-point diagnostic then reads a mostly monotone drift instead of actual profitability movements.

And the good news is even better:

your r_diag_real_net already looks economically plausible.

A median around 9–11 percent across subperiods is totally admissible as a diagnostic profit-rate object. That is the rate you should be using for swing identification.

The clean conceptual move is this:

keep r_struct_t as your structural profitability object

redefine r_diag_t as the real net diagnostic profit rate

keep the mixed current-price version only as a legacy audit variable, not as the main object

Why this is the right fix:

your structural object already isolates the price corridor through p_t

if the diagnostic rate also embeds asymmetric price repricing, it pollutes the comparison

using r_diag_real_net = (pi_t * GDP_real) / KNC keeps the diagnostic rate coherent with the net-capital denominator used in the structural decomposition

So yes: the builder should be patched again, but now in a very targeted way.

Use this patch in the profitability-construction section.

# ── 6. Build structural profitability objects ────────────────────────────────
d <- d |>
  dplyr::arrange(year) |>
  dplyr::mutate(
    # Relative-price corridor
    p_t = pY / pK,

    # Productive-capacity term
    B_t = Yp_hat / KGC,

    # Gross-to-net wedge
    nu_t = KGC / KNC,

    # Structural profitability
    r_struct_t    = pi_t * mu_t * p_t * B_t * nu_t,
    ln_r_struct_t = log(r_struct_t),

    # --- Diagnostic profitability candidates for audit ---
    GOS_real_t = pi_t * GDP_real,
    KNC_current_t = KNC * pK_sc,
    KGC_current_t = KGC * pK_sc,

    r_diag_real_net_t     = GOS_real_t / KNC,
    r_diag_real_gross_t   = GOS_real_t / KGC,
    r_diag_current_net_t  = GOS / KNC_current_t,
    r_diag_current_gross_t = GOS / KGC_current_t,

    # Freeze main diagnostic carrier on the coherent real-net rate
    r_diag_t    = r_diag_real_net_t,
    ln_r_diag_t = log(r_diag_t),

    # Log components
    ln_pi_t = log(pi_t),
    ln_mu_t = log(mu_t),
    ln_p_t  = log(p_t),
    ln_B_t  = log(B_t),
    ln_nu_t = log(nu_t),

    # Capital growth
    ln_KNC_t = log(KNC),
    g_K_t    = ln_KNC_t - dplyr::lag(ln_KNC_t),

    # Reproductive closure
    chi_t = dplyr::if_else(!is.na(GOS) & abs(GOS) > 1e-8, IGC / GOS, NA_real_),

    # Diagnostic wedge: structural vs coherent diagnostic rate
    accounting_wedge_t =
      dplyr::if_else(!is.na(r_diag_t) & abs(r_diag_t) > 1e-8, r_struct_t / r_diag_t, NA_real_),

    # Legacy mixed object kept only for audit
    r_diag_mixed_legacy_t = GOS / KNC
  )
Then also patch the admissibility check so it validates the new carrier explicitly:

required_profitability <- c(
  "r_struct_t", "r_diag_t", "r_diag_real_net_t",
  "p_t", "B_t", "nu_t", "chi_t"
)
And in the standalone diagnostic script, you can keep:

level_var <- "r_diag_t"
log_var   <- "ln_r_diag_t"
because after the builder patch those will now refer to the coherent real-net diagnostic rate.

One more thing matters here. Your audited results suggest that the right default diagnostic rate is the real-net one, not the current-net one. That is because your structural profitability already handles the relative-price corridor separately. So the diagnostic object should not reintroduce price distortions unless you want a separate explicit “nominal profitability” comparison.

So my recommendation is:

main diagnostic rate: r_diag_real_net_t

auxiliary audit rates:

r_diag_real_gross_t

r_diag_current_net_t

r_diag_current_gross_t

r_diag_mixed_legacy_t

That gives you a full audit trail without letting the bad series drive interpretation.

The workflow now should be:

patch the builder with the code above

rerun the builder

rerun the standalone diagnostic script

inspect whether the new fig01_chile_profit_turning_points_joint.png now shows actual internal profitability dynamics rather than that pancake-flat line

At this point, the flatness issue is no longer mysterious. It was a classic asymmetric repricing bug wearing a fake moustache.

    chi_t = dplyr::if_else(!is.na(GOS) & abs(GOS) > 1e-8, IGC / GOS, NA_real_),
    
    # Diagnostic wedge: structural vs coherent diagnostic rate
    accounting_wedge_t =
      dplyr::if_else(!is.na(r_diag_t) & abs(r_diag_t) > 1e-8, r_struct_t / r_diag_t, NA_real_),
    
    # Legacy mixed object kept only for audit
    r_diag_mixed_legacy_t = GOS / KNC
  )

if (any(d$r_struct_t <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("r_struct_t has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$r_diag_t <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) stop("r_diag_t has non-positive values.", call. = FALSE)
if (any(d$nu_t < 1, na.rm = TRUE)) warning("nu_t < 1 detected; inspect gross/net stock consistency.", call. = FALSE)

Thought for 1m 0s
This diagnostic is now doing something meaningful. It is no longer dominated by the scale bug from the mixed-rate construction. The profit-rate line now lives in a plausible range, roughly 8–14 percent, so the turning points are interpretable as actual profitability movements rather than as a price-level artifact. That matters because your locked rule for Chile is exactly this: keep the U.S.-style signal logic, but date turning points on the local extremum of the profit-rate series rather than on the derivative sign-change year alone. 


My reading is that the diagnostic gives you a decent long-wave structure, but it is still too coarse for the 1971–1973 critical juncture if you want that episode unpacked internally.

The first figure gives a clear medium-run sequence. I would read the detected swings as:
1940–1946 up, 1946–1949 down, 1949–1955 up, 1955–1961 down, 1961–1969 up, 1969–1975 down, and 1975–1978 up. That is a coherent alternation, and it is far better than the earlier flat object. What it says, though, is that the algorithm is picking up a major peak in 1969 and then a major trough only in 1975. So the whole UP period plus the immediate coup aftermath is being absorbed into one broad downward swing rather than split into “1971 offset → 1972 reversal → post-1973 forced offset.” That means the current smoothing/pruning setup is adequate for broad periodization, but not yet for the finer historical sequence you want. 😄

The second figure is even more interesting. ECT is high and positive in the 1940s, then trends downward through the 1950s, briefly recovers around the early 1960s, and then falls sharply negative after the early 1970s. In other words, the external disequilibrium indicator is not merely noisy background. It suggests a structural deterioration that becomes especially severe in the early-to-mid 1970s. That lines up well with your insistence that the profitability story cannot be read in isolation from balance-of-payments stress, because ect is explicitly carried into the merged Chile panel as part of the structural base. 


So the current joint reading is this.

At the broad level, profitability looks like it peaks before the UP phase and enters a major downswing that runs across the late 1960s into the mid-1970s. At the same time, the external imbalance indicator deteriorates strongly through the same general window. That gives you a plausible “twin stress” diagnosis: a profitability downswing coinciding with worsening external disequilibrium.

But at the fine historical level, the diagnostic still under-separates the critical juncture. Your own target sequence was: late-1960s breakdown, big UP offset in 1971, reversal starting in 1972, post-coup offset, and then an unsustained ending. 

 The current output does not yet give you that. It gives you instead:

a late-1960s / 1969 peak,
a broad contraction through 1975,
and then a recovery from 1975 to 1978.

That is historically intelligible, but it is too aggregated for the political sequence you want to narrate.

So the verdict is:

The diagnostic is now usable for medium-run structure. ✅
It is not yet sharp enough for the internal chronology of 1971–1973. ⚠️

Why that happens is straightforward. The signal is driven by smoothed Δ log(r) and then pruned with minimum-duration and minimum-log-move thresholds. That combination is exactly what should produce broader swings and suppress short internal reversals. In other words, the algorithm is currently behaving consistently with its own design. The problem is not malfunction now. The problem is resolution. Your builder history also shows why that distinction matters: earlier the core was mixing carriers between search and pruning, and the repair package explicitly moved toward cleaner separation and declared thresholds.

My practical assessment is this:

For descriptive periodization of profitability, this output is good enough to say:
there is a major profitability contraction from the late 1960s into the mid-1970s, with mounting external imbalance.

For historical reconstruction of the UP critical juncture, you need one additional pass:
run a second, explicitly “high-resolution” diagnostic for 1968–1976 only, with lighter smoothing and looser pruning, while keeping the full-sample diagnostic as the major-swing baseline.

That gives you two layers:
a full-sample major swing chronology, and
a focused critical-juncture chronology.

That is the cleanest architecture. It avoids making the full-sample algorithm do a job it is not tuned to do.

So, in plain terms: this diagnostic now tells a real story, and the story is already pretty strong. It says the late 1960s into the mid-1970s is a genuine crisis corridor where profitability and external imbalance worsen together. What it does not yet tell is the internal choreography of the UP years. That will need a narrower-window diagnostic rather than more argument about this one.

# ── 2. Helpers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
sign_eps <- function(x, eps = 1e-10) {
  ifelse(is.na(x) | abs(x) <= eps, 0L, ifelse(x > 0, 1L, -1L))
}

zsafe <- function(x) {
  s <- stats::sd(x, na.rm = TRUE)
  m <- mean(x, na.rm = TRUE)
  if (!is.finite(s) || s <= 0) return(rep(NA_real_, length(x)))
  (x - m) / s
}

load_profitability_panel <- function(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds) {
  if (file.exists(path_d_rds)) {
    return(readRDS(path_d_rds))
  }

  if (file.exists(path_bundle_rds)) {
    b <- readRDS(path_bundle_rds)
    if (!("d" %in% names(b))) {
      stop("Bundle found, but object 'd' is missing.", call. = FALSE)
    }
    return(b$d)
  }

  stop(
    "Could not find either d_merged_profitability_chile.rds or analytical_bundle_chile.rds.",
    call. = FALSE
  )
}

locate_local_extremum <- function(year, level, i, type, span = 1L) {
  lo <- max(1L, i - span)
  hi <- min(length(level), i + span)
  win_idx <- lo:hi
  win_val <- level[win_idx]

  if (all(is.na(win_val))) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      idx = i,
      year = year[i],
      value = level[i],
      type = type
    ))
  }

  j <- if (type == "peak") {
    win_idx[which.max(win_val)]
  } else {
    win_idx[which.min(win_val)]
  }

  tibble::tibble(
    idx = j,
    year = year[j],
    value = level[j],
    type = type
  )
}

compute_signal_table <- function(df, level_var, log_var, k_smooth,
                                 ect_var = "ect", ect_smooth_k = 3L) {
  if (!(level_var %in% names(df))) {
    stop("Missing level_var in input data: ", level_var, call. = FALSE)
  }
  if (!(ect_var %in% names(df))) {
    stop("Missing ect_var in input data: ", ect_var, call. = FALSE)
  }

  out <- df |>
    dplyr::arrange(year) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = .data[[level_var]],
      ln_r    = if (log_var %in% names(df)) .data[[log_var]] else log(.data[[level_var]]),
      ect     = .data[[ect_var]]
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r = ln_r - dplyr::lag(ln_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed = zoo::rollmean(dlog_r, k = k_smooth, fill = NA, align = "center"),
      ect_smoothed    = zoo::rollmean(ect, k = ect_smooth_k, fill = NA, align = "center")
    ) |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_r_z          = zsafe(dlog_r),
      dlog_r_smoothed_z = zsafe(dlog_r_smoothed),
      ect_z             = zsafe(ect),
      ect_smoothed_z    = zsafe(ect_smoothed)
    )

  out
}

compress_turning_points <- function(tp) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  keep <- vector("list", 0)
  current <- tp[1, , drop = FALSE]

  for (i in 2:nrow(tp)) {
    this <- tp[i, , drop = FALSE]

    if (this$type == current$type) {
      if (this$type == "peak"   && this$value > current$value) current <- this
      if (this$type == "trough" && this$value < current$value) current <- this
    } else {
      keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
      current <- this
    }
  }

  keep[[length(keep) + 1]] <- current
  dplyr::bind_rows(keep) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

find_tp_from_signal <- function(signal_tbl, signal_col, span = 1L, eps = 1e-10, method_name = "signal_rule") {
  year  <- signal_tbl$year
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl[[signal_col]]

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  if (length(sig) < 3) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  for (i in 2:(length(sig) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(sig[i - 1]) || is.na(sig[i])) next

    s_prev <- sign_eps(sig[i - 1], eps = eps)
    s_curr <- sign_eps(sig[i], eps = eps)

    if (s_prev > 0L && s_curr < 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "peak", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = method_name,
        signal_col = signal_col,
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    } else if (s_prev < 0L && s_curr > 0L) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "trough", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = method_name,
        signal_col = signal_col,
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = sig[i - 1],
        signal_curr = sig[i],
        signal_strength = abs(sig[i - 1]) + abs(sig[i])
      )
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

find_tp_from_levels <- function(signal_tbl, span = 1L) {
  year  <- signal_tbl$year
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level

  out <- vector("list", 0)

  if (length(level) < 3) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  for (i in 2:(length(level) - 1)) {
    if (is.na(level[i - 1]) || is.na(level[i]) || is.na(level[i + 1])) next

    if (level[i - 1] < level[i] && level[i] > level[i + 1]) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "peak", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = "level_extrema",
        signal_col = "r_level",
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = NA_real_,
        signal_curr = NA_real_,
        signal_strength = NA_real_
      )
    } else if (level[i - 1] > level[i] && level[i] < level[i + 1]) {
      ext <- locate_local_extremum(year, level, i, "trough", span = span)
      out[[length(out) + 1]] <- tibble::tibble(
        method = "level_extrema",
        signal_col = "r_level",
        signal_idx = i,
        signal_year = year[i],
        idx = ext$idx,
        year = ext$year,
        value = ext$value,
        type = ext$type,
        signal_prev = NA_real_,
        signal_curr = NA_real_,
        signal_strength = NA_real_
      )
    }
  }

  if (length(out) == 0) {
    return(tibble::tibble(
      method = character(),
      signal_col = character(),
      signal_idx = integer(),
      signal_year = integer(),
      idx = integer(),
      year = integer(),
      value = numeric(),
      type = character(),
      signal_prev = numeric(),
      signal_curr = numeric(),
      signal_strength = numeric()
    ))
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out) |>
    dplyr::distinct(idx, .keep_all = TRUE) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx)
}

prune_turning_points_joint <- function(tp, signal_tbl, min_years = 2L, min_log_move = 0.02) {
  if (nrow(tp) <= 1) return(tp)

  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  log_level <- log(level)
  out <- tp

  repeat {
    if (nrow(out) <= 1) break

    dur <- diff(out$year)
    amp_log <- abs(diff(log_level[out$idx]))
    weak <- which(dur < min_years | amp_log < min_log_move)

    if (length(weak) == 0) break

    k <- weak[1]

    if (k == 1) {
      out <- out[-2, , drop = FALSE]
    } else if (k == nrow(out) - 1) {
      out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
    } else {
      left_idx  <- out$idx[k - 1]
      a_idx     <- out$idx[k]
      b_idx     <- out$idx[k + 1]
      right_idx <- out$idx[k + 2]

      move_drop_left  <- abs(log_level[b_idx] - log_level[left_idx])
      move_drop_right <- abs(log_level[right_idx] - log_level[a_idx])

      if (move_drop_left >= move_drop_right) {
        out <- out[-k, , drop = FALSE]
      } else {
        out <- out[-(k + 1), , drop = FALSE]
      }
    }

    out <- compress_turning_points(out)
  }

  out
}

make_boundary_only_tp <- function(signal_tbl) {
  level_first <- signal_tbl$r_level[1]
  level_last  <- signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)]

  start_type <- if (level_last >= level_first) "trough" else "peak"
  end_type   <- if (start_type == "trough") "peak" else "trough"

  tibble::tibble(
    method = "boundary_only",
    signal_col = NA_character_,
    signal_idx = c(NA_integer_, NA_integer_),
    signal_year = c(NA_integer_, NA_integer_),
    idx = c(1L, nrow(signal_tbl)),
    year = c(signal_tbl$year[1], signal_tbl$year[nrow(signal_tbl)]),
    value = c(signal_tbl$r_level[1], signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)]),
    type = c(start_type, end_type),
    signal_prev = c(NA_real_, NA_real_),
    signal_curr = c(NA_real_, NA_real_),
    signal_strength = c(NA_real_, NA_real_)
  )
}

add_boundaries_keep_rhs <- function(tp, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp) == 0) {
    return(make_boundary_only_tp(signal_tbl))
  }

  first_type <- if (tp$type[1] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"
  last_type  <- if (tp$type[nrow(tp)] == "peak") "trough" else "peak"

  start_row <- tibble::tibble(
    method = "boundary",
    signal_col = NA_character_,
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = 1L,
    year = signal_tbl$year[1],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[1],
    type = first_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  end_row <- tibble::tibble(
    method = "boundary",
    signal_col = NA_character_,
    signal_idx = NA_integer_,
    signal_year = NA_integer_,
    idx = nrow(signal_tbl),
    year = signal_tbl$year[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    value = signal_tbl$r_level[nrow(signal_tbl)],
    type = last_type,
    signal_prev = NA_real_,
    signal_curr = NA_real_,
    signal_strength = NA_real_
  )

  dplyr::bind_rows(start_row, tp, end_row) |>
    dplyr::arrange(idx) |>
    compress_turning_points()
}

build_swing_table <- function(tp_bounds, signal_tbl) {
  if (nrow(tp_bounds) < 2) return(tibble::tibble())

  out <- vector("list", nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)

  for (i in seq_len(nrow(tp_bounds) - 1)) {
    idx0 <- tp_bounds$idx[i]
    idx1 <- tp_bounds$idx[i + 1]

    y0 <- tp_bounds$year[i]
    y1 <- tp_bounds$year[i + 1]

    r0  <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx0]
    r1  <- signal_tbl$r_level[idx1]
    ln0 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx0]
    ln1 <- signal_tbl$ln_r[idx1]

    ect0 <- signal_tbl$ect[idx0]
    ect1 <- signal_tbl$ect[idx1]
    ect_avg <- mean(signal_tbl$ect[idx0:idx1], na.rm = TRUE)
    ect_sm_avg <- mean(signal_tbl$ect_smoothed[idx0:idx1], na.rm = TRUE)

    dur <- y1 - y0

    out[[i]] <- tibble::tibble(
      swing_id = i,
      start_year = y0,
      end_year = y1,
      start_type = tp_bounds$type[i],
      end_type   = tp_bounds$type[i + 1],
      direction  = paste0(tp_bounds$type[i], "_to_", tp_bounds$type[i + 1]),
      duration_years = dur,
      start_r = r0,
      end_r   = r1,
      amplitude_pct = 100 * (r1 / r0 - 1),
      amplitude_log = ln1 - ln0,
      pace_pct_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, 100 * ((r1 / r0)^(1 / dur) - 1), NA_real_),
      pace_log_per_year = ifelse(dur > 0, (ln1 - ln0) / dur, NA_real_),
      ect_start = ect0,
      ect_end   = ect1,
      ect_avg   = ect_avg,
      ect_smoothed_avg = ect_sm_avg,
      boundary_only = all(tp_bounds$method == "boundary_only"),
      rhs_terminal_window = (i == (nrow(tp_bounds) - 1))
    )
  }

  dplyr::bind_rows(out)
}

plot_joint_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  level <- signal_tbl$r_level
  sig   <- signal_tbl$dlog_r_smoothed

  level_center <- mean(level, na.rm = TRUE)
  sig_range <- range(sig, na.rm = TRUE)
  lvl_range <- range(level, na.rm = TRUE)

  if (!all(is.finite(sig_range)) || diff(sig_range) == 0) {
    scale_fac <- 1
  } else {
    scale_fac <- 0.85 * diff(lvl_range) / diff(sig_range)
  }

  signal_plot <- signal_tbl |>
    dplyr::mutate(
      dlog_plot = level_center + dlog_r_smoothed * scale_fac
    )

  tp_plot <- tp_used |>
    dplyr::filter(!method %in% c("boundary", "boundary_only")) |>
    dplyr::transmute(
      year,
      r_level = value,
      type
    )

  p <- ggplot(signal_plot, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = level_center, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = r_level), linewidth = 1.1) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_plot), linetype = "dashed", linewidth = 0.9) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "peak"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2, stroke = 0.8, fill = NA
    ) +
    geom_point(
      data = dplyr::filter(tp_plot, type == "trough"),
      aes(y = r_level, shape = type),
      size = 3.2, stroke = 0.8, fill = NA
    ) +
    scale_shape_manual(values = c(peak = 24, trough = 25)) +
    scale_y_continuous(
      name = "profit rate",
      sec.axis = sec_axis(
        trans = ~ (. - level_center) / scale_fac,
        name = "smoothed Δ log profitability"
      )
    ) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      title = title_txt,
      shape = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height)

  invisible(p)
}

plot_ect_diagnostic <- function(signal_tbl, tp_used, out_png, out_pdf, title_txt = NULL) {
  tp_vlines <- tp_used |>
    dplyr::filter(!method %in% c("boundary", "boundary_only"))

  p <- ggplot(signal_tbl, aes(x = year)) +
    geom_hline(yintercept = 0, linetype = "dotted", linewidth = 0.4) +
    geom_line(aes(y = dlog_r_smoothed_z, linetype = "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_line(aes(y = ect_smoothed_z, linetype = "ECT external imbalance (z)"), linewidth = 1.0) +
    geom_vline(
      data = tp_vlines,
      aes(xintercept = year),
      linewidth = 0.35,
      alpha = 0.45
    ) +
    scale_linetype_manual(values = c(
      "Smoothed Δlog profitability (z)" = "dashed",
      "ECT external imbalance (z)" = "solid"
    )) +
    labs(
      x = NULL,
      y = "standardized diagnostic scale",
      title = title_txt,
      linetype = NULL
    ) +
    theme_minimal(base_size = 13) +
    theme(
      panel.grid.minor = element_blank(),
      legend.position = "bottom"
    )

  ggsave(out_png, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height, dpi = fig_dpi)
  ggsave(out_pdf, p, width = fig_width, height = fig_height)

  invisible(p)
}

d <- load_profitability_panel(path_d_rds, path_bundle_rds)

required_vars <- c("year", level_var, ect_var)
miss_vars <- required_vars[!required_vars %in% names(d)]
if (length(miss_vars) > 0) {
  stop("Missing required variable(s): ", paste(miss_vars, collapse = ", "), call. = FALSE)
}

d <- d |>
  dplyr::filter(year >= analysis_year_min, year <= analysis_year_max) |>
  dplyr::arrange(year)

if (!(log_var %in% names(d))) {
  d[[log_var]] <- log(d[[level_var]])
}

if (any(!is.finite(d[[level_var]]) | d[[level_var]] <= 0, na.rm = TRUE)) {
  stop("Profit-rate level series contains non-positive or non-finite values.", call. = FALSE)
}

# ── 4. Compute signals ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
signal_tbl <- compute_signal_table(
  df = d,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  ect_smooth_k = ect_smooth_k
)

# ── 5. Detection ladder ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
tp_candidates_primary <- find_tp_from_signal(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  signal_col = "dlog_r_smoothed",
  span = local_span,
  method_name = "smoothed_dlog_rule"
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_candidates_raw <- find_tp_from_signal(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  signal_col = "dlog_r",
  span = local_span,
  method_name = "raw_dlog_rule"
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_candidates_level <- find_tp_from_levels(
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
  span = local_span
) |>
  compress_turning_points()

tp_candidates_used <- tp_candidates_primary
candidate_method_used <- "smoothed_dlog_rule"

if (nrow(tp_candidates_used) == 0 && nrow(tp_candidates_raw) > 0) {
  tp_candidates_used <- tp_candidates_raw
  candidate_method_used <- "raw_dlog_rule"
}

if (nrow(tp_candidates_used) == 0 && nrow(tp_candidates_level) > 0) {
  tp_candidates_used <- tp_candidates_level
  candidate_method_used <- "level_extrema"
}

tp_final_pruned <- if (nrow(tp_candidates_used) > 0) {
  prune_turning_points_joint(
    tp = tp_candidates_used,
    signal_tbl = signal_tbl,
    min_years = min_years_between_tp,
    min_log_move = min_log_move
  ) |>
    compress_turning_points()
} else {
  tp_candidates_used
}

tp_used <- tp_final_pruned
used_boundary_only <- FALSE

if (nrow(tp_used) == 0) {
  tp_used <- make_boundary_only_tp(signal_tbl)
  used_boundary_only <- TRUE
}

tp_bounds <- if (used_boundary_only) {
  tp_used
} else {
  add_boundaries_keep_rhs(
    tp = tp_used,
    signal_tbl = signal_tbl
  )
}

swings_tbl <- build_swing_table(
  tp_bounds = tp_bounds,
  signal_tbl = signal_tbl
)

tp_status <- tibble::tibble(
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  n_candidates_primary = nrow(tp_candidates_primary),
  n_candidates_raw = nrow(tp_candidates_raw),
  n_candidates_level = nrow(tp_candidates_level),
  candidate_method_used = candidate_method_used,
  n_candidates_used = nrow(tp_candidates_used),
  n_after_prune = nrow(tp_final_pruned),
  used_boundary_only = used_boundary_only
)

config_tbl <- tibble::tibble(
  analysis_year_min = analysis_year_min,
  analysis_year_max = analysis_year_max,
  level_var = level_var,
  log_var = log_var,
  ect_var = ect_var,
  k_smooth = k_smooth,
  ect_smooth_k = ect_smooth_k,
  local_span = local_span,
  min_years_between_tp = min_years_between_tp,
  min_log_move = min_log_move
)

Thought for 1m 57s
This short-run diagnostic is much better. It now gives you a usable political-economic sequence for 1957–1978, but it still does not fully unpack the internal choreography of 1971–1973.

The good part first. The algorithm is behaving cleanly. It used the primary smoothed-Δlog rule, generated 5 primary candidates, and after pruning kept 3 internal turning points, so this is not a fallback artifact. The resulting dated turning points are:

1961 trough

1969 peak

1975 trough

That implies four swings:

1957–1961: contraction, about -29.8%

1961–1969: expansion, about +49.0%

1969–1975: contraction, about -19.9%

1975–1978: rebound, about +28.5%

That is actually a strong short-run structure. It gives you a very readable narrative of the long-sixties rise ending in a profitability peak around 1969, followed by a major downswing that runs across the UP years and the immediate counter-revolutionary aftermath, then a rebound after 1975. That is broadly compatible with your diagnostic rule and with the way you wanted Chile dated on local extrema rather than on raw sign-change years. 


So for the long sixties, this works well. The short-run zoom makes the 1961–1969 rise much clearer than the full 1940–1978 figure. The first figure reads as:

low point around 1961

sustained rise through the 1960s

profitability crest around 1969

downward regime through 1975

recovery after 1975

That is analytically useful because it says the rise of the UP to state power occurs after a long profitability upswing but inside a broader transition into deterioration.

Now the limitation. The 1969–1975 downswing is still too aggregated for your more demanding historical target. You wanted something closer to:

late-1960s breakdown,

a strong UP offset in 1971,

reversal beginning in 1972,

post-1973 forced offset,

then unsustained ending.

This short-run output still does not split that sequence internally. It absorbs the whole interval into one broad contraction from 1969 to 1975. So it is better than the medium-run figure for political narration, but it is still not enough to tell the internal UP chronology on its own. 


The second figure is where things get really interesting. The ECT line and the profitability signal are not simply moving together. My reading is:

around 1960–1961, ECT is relatively strong while profitability momentum is weak or negative;

through the mid-to-late 1960s, profitability momentum improves and the level profit rate rises, but ECT does not strengthen in the same way;

after 1973, ECT collapses sharply into strongly negative territory, while profitability shows short-lived recovery impulses.

That divergence matters a lot. It suggests that even when profitability gets short-run offsets, the external disequilibrium constraint is worsening. In substantive terms: you may have domestic or political mechanisms generating temporary profitability relief, but they are being undermined by a deteriorating balance-of-payments position. That is exactly the kind of “forced offset under external stress” reading that makes the twin-crisis framing attractive.

So the short-run diagnostic gives you two strong takeaways.

First, for presentation, it is already good enough to support a major arc:
1961–1969 rise → 1969–1975 crisis corridor → 1975–1978 rebound.

Second, for interpretation, it strongly suggests that the post-1973 movement should not be read as a clean stabilization, because the ECT line is still deteriorating hard through the mid-1970s. The rebound in profitability looks more like a fragile or coercively induced offset than like a resolved regime repair.

My recommendation on presentation is now pretty clear.

Use the medium-run diagnostic to establish the long arc of accumulation and deterioration.

Use this 1957–1978 short-run diagnostic as the political-historical zoom for:

the long-sixties ascent,

the transition into crisis,

and the onset of counter-revolution.

But do not make this short-run figure carry the full burden of narrating 1971–1973 internally. It still does not separate that interval finely enough.

So the next decision is not whether this figure is useful. It is. The decision is whether you want one more, even tighter layer for the critical juncture itself. My answer is yes: for the UP sequence, you likely still need a micro-diagnostic window around 1968–1975 with lighter pruning, while keeping this 1957–1978 output as the more stable short-run backbone.



So the next decision is not whether this figure is useful. It is. The decision is whether you want one more, even tighter layer for the critical juncture itself. My answer is yes: for the UP sequence, you likely still need a **micro-diagnostic window around 1968–1975** with lighter pruning, while keeping this 1957–1978 output as the more stable short-run backbone.
